Current Commentary

Prospects for Currency Management

— Duan

It has been four days since the government managed the currency and centralized cash. In the past three days, although the market is still uneasy, there has been no panic or disturbance as before the announcement. The financial situation is gradually stabilizing. However, ordinary family life suddenly feels that "foreign prices are low, but domestic prices are high." This is indeed a temporary phenomenon. There is no reform without pain. After a series of changes, we should seek industrial recovery and price stability, so that life is enjoyable. Why should we hesitate to endure temporary pain? However, if prices rise and purchasing power cannot keep up, resulting in a situation where higher prices lead to weaker purchasing power, it is also worrying. Some say that this will never happen. As prices rise and production develops, how can purchasing power not increase? It should be noted that among the majority of Chinese people who only seek enjoyment and do not engage in production, the occurrence of this unfortunate phenomenon is quite possible. Thereafter, if the financial activities focus solely on supporting the real estate industry, how much benefit will it bring to the overall issue of industrial recovery? It is questionable. If real estate speculation were to revive, what benefits would it bring to industrialists and businessmen? It is not difficult to know by looking back.

However, if our country's finances follow the past, without major changes, the exchange rate will be stable, prices will be stable, speculation in foreign exchange will be reduced, and funds for legitimate businesses will be available. Everything may gradually get on the right track. However, this still requires great effort.

China has a vast territory, and the success of a reform is not as easy as in other countries. However, without external destruction, there will eventually be a day of success. British banks have been ordered by their government to cooperate with us. Although the US government is unwilling to indicate whether it will advise American overseas Chinese to cooperate with the Chinese government, it has stated that it will continue its previous promises to China and do its best to avoid interfering with the Chinese government's recent efforts to stabilize the currency. It is unwilling to disrupt world silver prices during this period. It can be seen that the United States is at least willing to cooperate indirectly. However, Japan has not yet made a clear statement. If what its embassy has said is true, that the Japanese government will cancel its positive attitude towards whether Japanese banks in China will cooperate with us and is unwilling to guarantee them, then this is something to be deeply regretted. China and Japan are seeking friendship, and Japan should assist China's legitimate reforms. Moreover, a stable exchange rate is beneficial to trade between the two countries. Why does it still hold narrow-minded views and attempt to monopolize, and become uneasy because the Japanese exchange rate has fallen from 130 or 140 yuan to 103 yuan?

Before the centralization of silver, smuggling was rampant in Tianjin, Qingdao, Jinan, Shanghai, Xiamen, and other places. According to the price of silver in London, the value of one yuan is still more than 60% of its face value. Where there is great profit, it is hard to guarantee that there will be no organized trafficking. This is indeed a great obstacle to our current silver centralization. Now, a difficult task is placed on the shoulders of our Chinese people. People are using our ability to overcome all difficulties, dispel suspicions, and maintain credit as a standard for observing the future of our country's currency. How can we be complacent and not know how to encourage ourselves?

Continuing Discussions Between Britain and Italy to Ease Mediterranean Tensions

Rome Publishes Communiqué, Talks Friendly; Italian Troop Withdrawal Conditioned on British Ship Withdrawal

(Rome) Prime Minister Mussolini received British Ambassador Sir Drummond in the afternoon and subsequently issued an official communiqué stating that the meeting involved discussions on the Anglo-Italian situation in the Mediterranean. According to this newspaper's correspondent, the two men explored ways to improve relations between the two countries. Drummond requested that Italy continue to withdraw troops stationed in Libya. The two also discussed the upcoming London Naval Conference, with particular emphasis on the basis for a new naval balance in the Mediterranean. According to semi-official sources, Mussolini stated to Drummond that Italy had already withdrawn one division of troops from Libya, while Drummond explained that Britain still did not have grounds to reduce its naval vessels in the Mediterranean. The general public had a favorable impression of the talks, and political circles pointed out that although the repeated meetings between the Italian Prime Minister and the British Ambassador had not outwardly yielded concrete results, they were bound to bring about progress in the Italo-Abyssinian dispute. (Havas, 5th)

(Rome) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and British Ambassador Drummond continued their discussions on the Mediterranean situation today, but without any resolution. According to a communiqué, Mr. Mussolini mentioned that Italy had withdrawn one division of Italian troops from Libya, after which Drummond expressed the British government's admiration for this action. However, he stated that the number of Italian troops stationed in Libya still outnumbered the British and Egyptian troops in Egypt by approximately three times, and therefore the British government did not believe that this situation warranted the withdrawal of British naval vessels from the Mediterranean. The presence of the British fleet in the Mediterranean was purely for precautionary purposes. The talks were generally friendly, but the Italian side's spokesperson did not express excessive optimism. (Reuters, 5th)

Italian Prime Minister Advocates Expanding Scope of Talks; Demands Naval Parity in Mediterranean

(London) It is reported that during a meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and British Ambassador Sir Drummond in Rome today, they discussed steps that could be taken to ease tensions in the Mediterranean. Regarding this matter, well-informed sources explained that if Italian newspapers continued to engage in anti-British propaganda, and if the Italian troops stationed in Libya did not withdraw another division, Britain would not reduce the number of its naval vessels in the Mediterranean. However, if Italy were to comply, Britain not only intended to recall the two large battleships "Hotspur" and "Renown" to their home country, but might also recall a squadron of cruisers and torpedo boats. It is rumored that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini intends to expand the scope of the talks and raise the issue of naval parity in the Mediterranean for discussion. Regarding this matter, official circles stated that the only current issue was restoring peace in Africa, and nothing else was under consideration. Although naval experts from Britain and Italy were scheduled to begin talks tomorrow, their nature would also be strictly limited to preparations for the naval conference to be held on December 2nd. (Havas, 5th)

Italy Agrees to Further Withdrawal of Libyan Troops; Anglo-French Cooperation in Negotiations Sees Progress

(London) According to the Daily Mail and the Daily Express, regarding the troop withdrawal issue between Britain and Italy, if Italy agreed to reduce the number of troops stationed in Libya, there was a possibility that Britain's navy stationed in the Mediterranean might withdraw two or even more warships. Prime Minister Baldwin convened several cabinet members yesterday for discussion. According to the News Chronicle, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini had already accepted the further withdrawal of two divisions of troops stationed in Libya, bringing the total number of troops withdrawn to 30,000, but on the condition that Britain recall several warships stationed in the Mediterranean. Regarding this matter, the Morning Post believed that Britain would not consider reducing the number of naval vessels in the Mediterranean until the issue of naval cooperation with France had reached complete agreement. According to reports, French naval experts Admiral Darlan and Colonel Roux had come to Britain to discuss the cooperation issue, and significant progress had been made. Only a few points remained unresolved. (Havas, 6th)

Britain Harboring Three Types of Fears; Employing Strategies to Alienate Italy and France

(Rome) According to official sources here, the main purpose of the negotiations currently being conducted by Britain and Italy outside the League of Nations is not to resolve the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, but to resolve the difficult situation in the Mediterranean. A prominent figure here recently expressed to a Havas reporter that "After the outbreak of the Italo-Abyssinian dispute, the British government adopted an unprecedentedly harsh attitude towards Italy, which was due to three types of fears harbored by Britain. First, it was deeply concerned that after Italy succeeded in Abyssinia, it would train an army of 500,000 Abyssinian troops between British Egypt and the British Sudan and the Red Sea, making it the most powerful army in Africa. Second, it was afraid that the Italian navy would continue to develop. Third, it was afraid that the friendship between France and Italy would increasingly improve, thereby endangering Britain. Because of these three types of fears, Britain urged the League of Nations to take the strongest possible action to prevent Italy's power from extending into Abyssinia, and Italy has always believed that Britain's original intention was to take military sanctions. Britain believed that only by using naval pressure on Italy could Britain's three types of fears be completely dispelled. Later, because the military sanctions policy failed to gain the agreement of all countries, it failed. Britain then turned to negotiations, hoping to seek compensation in two areas: creating a balance of power in the Mediterranean and alienating Franco-Italian relations. According to this newspaper's correspondent, the British government is indeed currently pursuing the above-mentioned policy. If Britain and Italy can reach a compromise on the Mediterranean issue, then the Abyssinian problem will not be difficult to solve." (Havas, 6th)

British Navy Plans to Establish New Base in Mediterranean; British and Italian Experts Hold Talks in London in Preparation for Future Naval Conference

(Rome) According to the London correspondent of the Tribune, the British Admiralty plans to discuss with Italian naval experts the establishment of a new system of British naval bases in the Mediterranean to protect the Suez Canal and the Mosul oil pipeline in case of unforeseen events. Currently, the British navy's main bases in the Mediterranean are the Strait of Gibraltar and Malta, which are both very far from Singapore. According to the proposed new system, the British fleet could be concentrated in the eastern Mediterranean, which is closer to Singapore. According to the correspondent, the British navy has already been building new bases near the Suez Canal and the Red Sea, such as on Perim Island, so the above plan is already being implemented. (Havas, 5th)

(London) Italian naval experts, including Rear Admiral Piscia and Captain Magguttini, arrived here this evening and will hold talks with British experts in preparation for the future naval conference. Officials stated that these talks are absolutely unrelated to the current situation in the Mediterranean. (Havas, 5th)

League of Nations Economic Sanctions Against Italy; Expansion of Scope of Embargoed Goods; Oil, Coal, and Steel All Included in Embargo List; 18-Member Committee to Present for Discussion

(Geneva) The 18-member committee will present concrete proposals tonight to ban the transport of oil, coal and steel to Italy. It is now expected that when enough countries have approved of the proposal to make it effective, it will be decided when to implement it. The main business of today's committee will be to consider the reports of the five-member subcommittee regarding discussions of various technical issues arising from the implementation of sanctions. Eden and others have returned home to campaign for elections, so British Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs, Stanhope, will arrive in Geneva today to represent the British government at the meeting of the 18-member committee. (Reuters, 6th)

(Geneva) General agreement has been reached today on various outstanding issues regarding the implementation of sanctions against Italy, such as the difficulties of transit, clearing contracts and currency contracts. The 18-member committee will be able to approve the resolutions established by the subcommittees when it meets tonight. The transit subcommittee has found a solution today to the problem of preventing major items from being transported to other countries and then to Italy in order to circumvent the ban. The subcommittee maintains that countries participating in the sanctions need not apply quotas, but that member states must find ways to manage the destinations of prohibited goods. (Reuters, 6th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Economic Sanctions Subcommittee today passed a resolution stipulating that, starting November 18, steel, oil, coal and iron will also be added to the list of major products embargoed against Italy. However, this requires cooperation from Germany and the United States. The proposal was made by the Canadian representative at today's meeting, at which the Chilean representative opposed it, calling it impractical. Most diplomats here said that US law could not prohibit the export of these four items, and that if the League of Nations passed this resolution, it would be asking for the US to reject it. However, those who supported the proposal believed that Italian aircraft might not be able to fly due to lack of gasoline, so it might be worth a try. Furthermore, Italian tanks would not be able to move forward without oil, Italian ships would not be able to sail without coal, and various arms industries would come to a standstill without steel, as Italy's war machine relied entirely on other countries for raw materials. (National Society, 5th)

(Geneva) The Economic Sanctions Committee of the 18-Nation Committee recently discussed the draft resolution submitted by the Barter Issues Subcommittee, stipulating that all governments should cease to implement barter agreements with Italy no later than November 18, and that from that date onwards, the acceptance of deposits in various Italian currencies for the purpose of paying for exports to Italy should be prohibited. After discussion, the Dutch representative submitted an amendment, and the committee decided to send the original draft resolution, along with the amendment, to the subcommittee for reconsideration. (Havas, 5th)

British Give Unusual Importance to Oil Embargo Plan; Believe That It Cannot Succeed Without US and German Cooperation

(London) Political figures here attach great importance to the League of Nations' plan to embargo oil against Italy. According to an investigation of 1934, Italy's oil refining consumption reached 422,000 tons, gas oil consumption reached 226,000 tons, lubricating oil consumption reached 251,000 tons, and gasoline consumption reached 1.63 million tons. Since the military action, the consumption of various oils has increased even more. If the source of oil to Italy is to be cut off, it will not succeed without the United States banning oil transport. But apart from implementing a blockade against Italy to prevent American oil from entering, it is questionable whether the United States is willing to participate in the embargo. Even if the United States participates in the embargo, other countries can transport kerosene through Austria to enter Italy (because Austria has not participated in the sanctions). If this is the case, then the embargo on oil against Italy may be difficult to achieve. In addition, Albania provides Italy with approximately 500,000 tons of crude oil each year, the quality of which is equivalent to that produced in Romania. Italian oil companies enjoy the concession rights to the oil wells in Sissesarani and Divoli in Albania, and the oil produced is transported through a 70-kilometer pipeline to the Adriatic coast near Fiero, and then transported to Italy. (Havas, 5th)

Italy Employs Thrift to Resist Economic Sanctions; Soaring Oil Prices Cause Public Complaints

(Rome) Starting today, Italy is adopting various strict measures nationwide to resist economic sanctions against Italy. Butcher shops in various places will be closed for two days today and tomorrow to reduce meat consumption. People across the country will uniformly advance their living time by one hour to reduce electricity consumption. Except for electric railways, trains in various places will reduce the number of runs to save coal used by the railways. Foreign films and foreign books and newspapers will be uniformly boycotted. (Havas, 6th)

(Rome) Today, the price of gasoline in Italy has risen from 51 pence per gallon to 64 pence. The price two months ago was 34 pence. According to orders from the authorities, the price increase is for the purpose of saving, but in reality, it is affected by the League of Nations' sanctions. Motorists in particular have many complaints about this. (Havas, 6th)

Naval Conference Postponed; Opening Changed to December 5

(London) The naval conference originally scheduled to open here on December 2 has now been changed to December 5 because the Japanese representative is unable to arrive in London in time. (Reuters, 6th)

(London) The London Naval Conference, originally scheduled to open on December 2, has now been postponed to December 5 because the Japanese government informed the United States that the Japanese representatives attending the Naval Conference could not arrive in London before December 4. Therefore, Britain decided to postpone the conference to December 5. Furthermore, the French government's official reply accepting participation in the Naval Conference was delivered to London today. At the same time, the Indian government has also agreed to send representatives to the conference. (Havas, 6th)

Page 6

Italian Troops in the North Advance in the Rain

Vanguard Once Entered Magal City; Abyssinian Army Counterattacks at Night to Repel Enemy

Abyssinia, Special Correspondent for this Newspaper, O'Shaughnessy, reports: The Abyssinian government issued a communiqué late yesterday, officially announcing that a vanguard team of Italian troops had once entered the city of Magal. After the Abyssinian army launched a night counterattack, they forced the Italian troops to withdraw from the city. In this battle, ten Italian soldiers were killed and four captured. Two Abyssinian soldiers were killed and two wounded. At present, Magal City is still in the hands of the Abyssinian army. As for the southern town of Gorahei, it was bombed by Italian planes, injuring seven Abyssinian soldiers. Italian troops also attacked Abyssinian guard posts near the Webe Shebelle River. After fierce resistance, the Abyssinian army was forced to retreat. According to this newspaper's special correspondent, Italian troops will soon launch a large-scale offensive against Magal City, but the Abyssinian army has transported a batch of military supplies from abroad and is now stepping up preparations to resist. (Havas, 6th)

(Rome) According to semi-official sources today, heavy rain has hampered the Italian army's progress, especially for the heavy artillery units. However, this obstacle is not expected to disrupt the Italian army's plans. (National News Agency, 5th)

Italian Troops at the Northern Front: Although heavy rain has prevented Italian troops from attacking Magal, they will continue to advance after the road construction is completed and military supplies are delivered. The weather impeding the Italian army is completely abnormal, with thick clouds and heavy rain, even causing the Italian soldiers to fear the cold. The territory now occupied by the Italian army has increased by 4,300 square miles. The town of Ho-Hsing, captured yesterday, is an important junction where five camel routes converge. (National News Agency, 5th)

Asmara: Despite the extremely harsh weather, Italian troops at the northern front continued to advance today toward their main target, Magal. In the afternoon, they advanced to Agra, 16 miles north of the city. The troops advancing from Adigrat, Adowa, and Axum are scheduled to meet here. It is now expected that the main force of the Italian army will occupy Magal on Sunday. There was a heavy thunderstorm today, and the mountainsides became torrents. The Italian troops traveled on rugged paths with great difficulty, but the soldiers still marched in the rain all day long. By the time they reached Agra, they were soaked to the skin. The Italian army uses more than 7,000 mules, donkeys, and camels to transport food to the forward positions. There are also hundreds of trucks shuttling back and forth. It is reported that the bishop of Magal City has raised a white flag and it is expected that the entire clergy will surrender to the Italian army. Taigas, the chairman of the Agam region, surrendered to the Italian army headquarters today. It is expected that more minor chairmen will continue to surrender. The previous rumor that the wife and family members of Abyssinian commander Kufsa, who had surrendered to the Italian army, had all been slaughtered has not been verified. Well-informed sources indicate that this statement is completely unfounded. (Reuters, 6th)

Wogga Garden Front: Abyssinian Army Fortifies Positions

King Prepares to Depart for Personal Command; Northern Strategy Lures Enemy Deep

Abyssinia: Today, twenty cargo trucks loaded with various materials drove to Taishi City to repair the bridges that were destroyed by floods for two seasons, so that when the Abyssinian Emperor went on a personal expedition, the large army could pass through. It is reported that the Abyssinian Emperor will have 500 donkeys carrying butter, wine, military supplies and silk money. According to private sources, the Abyssinian army has built strong fortifications on the Wogga Garden front and is preparing to fight when the Italian army attacks. (Havas, 5th)

Abyssinia: Some officials here stated today that although Abyssinia had previously stated that it did not intend to resist the Italian army's advance, Magal would still be defended. According to the plans of the Abyssinian Army, the defending army will not resist with all its strength, because Magal is not important in practice. Therefore, the Abyssinian army will wait until they reach a more important location before deciding on a victory or defeat. Abyssinia's slight resistance is apparently to appease the chiefs who are strongly advocating open warfare. Prince Makonnen will probably arrive here from Taishi within two or three days, after which the Abyssinian Emperor will personally go to the northern front. (National News Agency, 5th)

League of Nations Financial Assistance Hopeless; Abyssinia Raises Domestic Public Debt

Haile Selassie Donates Large Sums as Advocate; Large Batch of Military Supplies to Arrive Successively

Abyssinia, Special Correspondent for this Newspaper, O'Shaughnessy, reports: The Abyssinian Emperor recently adopted the suggestion of Haile Selassie, the former representative to the League of Nations and minister to France, to raise public debt throughout the country to fund the war effort. Haile Selassie was the first to donate a large sum of money and a piece of real estate to encourage others. Haile Selassie also plans to personally go to the Qalqel region tomorrow to sell all of his farm's harvests to replenish the country's treasury. According to officials, Abyssinia's request to the League of Nations for financial assistance is bound to be rejected, so it intends to raise public debt domestically instead. Furthermore, the Abyssinian government will soon prohibit the import of various Italian goods, with alcohol and automobiles being the largest categories. After various countries lifted their orders to stop the transport of military supplies to Abyssinia, a large batch of military supplies will arrive successively. Government officials are contacting representatives of military supply companies in various countries every day to place orders. In addition, the government will purchase a large batch of radio materials to increase the number of mobile military radio stations. (Havas, 5th)

Egypt Actively Deploys Defenses

Heavy Artillery Placed on Mountain Peaks; Auto Stations Built Posthaste

Cairo: The Egyptian government has taken important defensive measures. Heavy artillery has been deployed on the peaks of mountains near Suleim, and anti-aircraft guns have been installed. At the same time, the city of Marsa Matruh has also been fortified, as troops and military supplies will be concentrated in the city. Transportation agencies are busy repairing roads in the western desert. In addition, the government has allocated 100,000 pounds to build a car road from Cairo to Alexandria, which is 300 kilometers long. This road passes through Wadi and Natrun, which is of great benefit to local chemical industries in these areas, especially salt and nitrate products. Furthermore, 45 British warships recently set sail from Alexandria to participate in air force exercises. (Havas, 6th)

Haas' Remains Funeralized

Diplomats from Various Countries Give Final Respects; Eulogy from Avenol Praises Deeds and Continuation

(Geneva) Haas, Director of the League of Nations Transportation Department, passed away the day before yesterday due to a heart attack. The funeral ceremony was held here this afternoon. Haas is the first director of the League of Nations to die in office. (Havas, 5th)

(Geneva) Dr. Haas, Director of the League of Nations Transportation Department, passed away here on Sunday. Today, his remains were placed in the League of Nations Assembly Hall, which was covered in black crepe, and will be buried in Paris. Friends and diplomats all walked into the hall one after another to pay their final respects. Secretary-General Avenol gave a brief eulogy, praising his report on China as being full of prudent considerations and correct judgments. Dr. Haas traveled to China earlier this year as a consultant for the League of Nations, spending several months there. He conducted careful research on the difficulties of China's construction and reform, and his report was recently published. (Reuters, 5th)

Minister of Finance Kung and Ambassador Knatchbull-Hugessen Issue Statement: British Loan to China is Untrue

Tokyo Government Expresses Satisfaction; British Ambassador to Japan Visits Hirota

(Tokyo) According to official sources today, Japanese Ambassador to China, Arima, met with Chinese Minister of Finance Kung Hsiang-hsi and British Ambassador Knatchbull-Hugessen, both of whom denied rumors of a British loan of 10 million pounds. Minister of Finance Kung stated to Arima that China would never borrow foreign debt to promote its new currency system. The Japanese government is said to be extremely satisfied with the statements of Minister of Finance Kung and the British Ambassador. Observers here, in light of past facts, firmly believe that Britain would never grant a loan to China without first consulting Japan. (Reuters, 6th)

(Tokyo) British Ambassador to Japan, Clive, visited Foreign Minister Hirota at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 6th. (Nichi-Nichi Allied, 6th)

Japanese Ministry of Finance to Send Personnel to China to Study Currency Reform

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Finance has decided to send Takeo Yumoto, Director of the Treasury Division of the Financial Bureau, and Masamichi Yamagiwa, Official of the Banking Bureau, to North China and Shanghai to study the issue of Chinese currency reform. (Nichi-Nichi Allied, 6th)

British and American Observations: Chinese Currency Stabilized; Joining the Sterling Bloc Premature

(London) Financial circles here are very supportive of China's move to devalue its currency by 40 percent, believing that a 40 percent devaluation is in line with the rate of devaluation of the pound sterling after Britain abandoned the gold standard. Some people believe that after the devaluation of the Chinese currency, it will join the pound sterling bloc, but it seems too early to make such an interpretation at present. Generally, it is believed that the decision taken by the Nanjing government this time is based on the monetary experience of most countries in recent years. Its intention is primarily to protect domestic silver reserves, second, to create a sound and stable monetary organization, and third, to protect the Chinese economy from foreign competition. As for joining the Sterling Bloc, it has not yet been considered. (Havas, 5th)

(Washington) Senior officials and financial experts here believe that the Chinese government's nationalization of silver has gradually stabilized Chinese currency. In theory, it can promote trade relations between China and the United States, but it still depends on other components of this new policy to succeed. Businesses, because they can predict that exchange rates will no longer fluctuate, will of course carefully consider their interests. Furthermore, the Chinese side has long advocated that stable silver prices are more valuable than rising prices. However, the flow of capital and price reactions are very important for trade. The State Department and the Treasury Department stated again today that the United States has no immediate response to this. (National News Agency, 5th)

(Washington) The Washington Post stated in an editorial today regarding the Chinese government's nationalization of silver, "American silver senators have shamelessly stated that high silver prices can increase China's purchasing power. Now, they are not ashamed to attribute the results of this assistance to China and the restoration of silver prices." (National News Agency, 5th)

Golden Rivers Flowing into America

Inflation Crisis Looms – Citibank Issues Warning

(New York) Citibank today reiterated its warning regarding potential credit inflation following the increase in domestic gold reserves. According to the bank's trade investigation report, if gold inflows into the United States exceed $475,000,000 in December, and concerning the excess reserves of the Federal Reserve Banks, this excess is neither normal nor sound, and a decline in currency value would be dangerous. The opportunity for inflation is already present. This can be seen by observing the gold inflows during the European war and the consequences of the Reserve Bank's currency purchase policy in 1927. The bank also believes that the unbalanced Federal government budget is a contributing factor to inflation. If the budget cannot be balanced, the authorities will find it difficult to curb inflation. If the Treasury Department raises funds from the market, the Federal Reserve Board will not have the freedom to act. (5th National Telegram)

Head of US Economic Survey Mission – Opinions on China's Currency Policy

The head of the American Far East Economic Survey Mission, Forbes, stated today that the written opinions submitted by Chinese bankers during the mission's visit to China foreshadowed the Chinese government's intention to nationalize silver. Regarding the future participation of the United States in the Chinese market, Forbes expressed optimism, differing significantly from the skepticism and pessimism of others. He stated that the mission members discovered many opportunities for Sino-American cooperation to restore China's finances and industries. (5th National Telegram)

(6th Chinese United Press Telegram)

Japanese-Manchukuo Troops Invade Russian Territory – Full Text of Soviet Protest to Japan

Kwantung Army Fully Responsible for Manchurian Defense – Japanese Government Cannot Shirk Responsibility for Disputes

(Moscow) On October 16th and 24th, the Soviet Ambassador to Japan, Yurenev, protested to the Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota regarding the intrusion of armed Manchurian troops into Soviet territory in the Grodekovo region on October 6th, 8th, and 12th. On the 25th, Hirota submitted a reply. On November 4th, Yurenev submitted the following memorandum to Hirota:

"The point raised in Your Excellency's memorandum that the Soviet border guards engaged in illegal acts during the clashes on October 6th and 12th is entirely unfounded and is therefore rejected by the Soviet government. I have already stated in my memorandum of October 16th and 14th that these clashes occurred within Soviet territory and were caused by the illegal intrusion of Japanese-Manchukuo armed forces into Soviet territory and their attack on Soviet border guards. Your Excellency's memorandum of October 25th does not deny that these incidents occurred within Soviet territory.

"Your Excellency also stated that the Japanese-Manchukuo armed forces were present at the scene for the sole purpose of investigation. This point must also be rejected, as the Japanese-Manchukuo troops have no right to conduct investigations within Soviet territory. Furthermore, the claim that the Soviet guards opened fire on the Japanese-Manchukuo troops without warning is also untrue. The Soviet patrol team, consisting of two cavalrymen, first warned the Japanese-Manchukuo troops who had intruded into Soviet territory. The latter not only did not leave Soviet territory but also opened fire on the Soviet border guards, resulting in the death of Guard Kotnikov and injuries to the other two. In this situation, the Soviet guards were obligated to follow service regulations and open fire on the Japanese-Manchukuo troops who had intruded into the country and attacked them. Therefore, Your Excellency's protest against the actions of the Soviet border guards is completely unfounded. At the outset of the incident, the Soviet government knew that the fault lay with the Japanese-Manchukuo side, but it still sought to convince the Japanese government of this fact. Therefore, it suggested that both countries immediately send representatives to form a joint commission to investigate the incident at the site. The Soviet government must express its regret that the Japanese government believes that an investigation by a joint commission is unnecessary. In fact, this method is the best guarantee of impartial and accurate fact-finding. I am instructed by the Soviet government to remind Your Excellency that the Japanese government has not yet responded to the draft proposal submitted by me on August 17th for the establishment of a joint Soviet-Manchukuo border commission. This proposal would provide a practical way to quickly investigate border disputes similar to the clash on October 12th and prevent such disputes, which disrupt border tranquility and peace, from recurring.

Your Excellency also stated that the cause of such disputes lies in the unclear demarcation of the Soviet-Manchukuo border. This point is also completely untrue. The Soviet-Manchukuo border was long ago agreed upon in a treaty signed by China and Russia, with an attached map for clarification. Upon the establishment of Manchukuo, it declared that such treaties must still be observed. There can be no doubt about the border established by these treaties. Before the entry of Japanese troops into Manchuria, such disputes never occurred.

"Finally, the Japanese government believes that this matter should be addressed to the Manchukuo government. The Soviet government must express its disagreement on this point. The Soviet government has repeatedly drawn the Japanese government's attention to the fact that the Japanese government cannot evade responsibility for any actions taken by the Japanese-Manchukuo authorities against the Soviet Union, as the military deployment in Manchuria is entirely carried out by Japan, and the Kwantung Army is the de facto ruler of Manchuria. At the same time, any consequences of the Soviet-Manchukuo border disputes will directly affect Soviet-Japanese relations. Furthermore, in this incident, as Your Excellency has stated, Japanese soldiers participated in this clash within the Japanese-Manchukuo forces. This fact alone proves that Japan is a party to this incident. At the same time, Your Excellency's recognition that the Soviet side opened fire on the Japanese-Manchukuo troops without provocation and should be protested also proves that Japan initially could not exclude itself from this incident. For all these reasons, the Soviet government considers its protest of October 24th to be entirely justified." (5th TASS Telegram)

Wang Jingwei's Condition Improving – Dictated Statements and Reports Yesterday

Recorded by Zeng Zhongming, Signed by Wang while Leaning on Pillow – Requesting Vice President Kong to Serve as Acting President

(Nanjing) President Wang's condition is steadily improving. The swelling on his left cheek has significantly subsided, and his appetite has increased. This morning, the 6th, he read newspapers and listened to those around him recite poetry and other literary works. Chiang Kai-shek, Lin Sen, and others who visited him to offer their condolences were all received and spoke to him in his room. This morning, he dictated a statement to Zeng Zhongming and a report requesting Vice President Kong to legally serve as Acting President. Both were recorded by Zeng and signed by Wang while leaning on his pillow. They have been verbally reported to the Executive Yuan meeting this afternoon by Chu and distributed to various newspapers. The original text is as follows: (1) "Due to injuries, Zhaoming cannot perform his duties and Vice President Kong should legally serve as Acting President." Reported to the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government. Note: Zhaoming, November 6th, 24th year. (2) "Since Zhaoming was injured, he has received warm care and visits from relatives, friends, and comrades, for which he is deeply grateful. Now that it is known that the injury is not fatal and that he has received treatment from famous doctors, he should not die. However, lying in bed and wasting working time is shameful. I will wait for my illness to be cured before offering my thanks." Respectfully conveyed, please understand. Note: Zhaoming, dictated from pillow, November 6th. Also, hospital report: morning and afternoon temperature 37 degrees, pulse 80, respiration 18. (6th Central News Agency Telegram)

He slept for nine hours on the night of the 5th, which was extremely comfortable. His temperature in the morning of the 6th was still 37 degrees, his pulse was 80, and his respiration was 17. He continues to consume liquid foods such as eggs and milk, and his appetite has increased significantly. Dr. Noel is attending to him at his bedside at all times. Chairman Chiang's Letter to Wang Shijie – Rectifying Student Discipline

Hats Must Be Straight, Clothes Must Be Tight, So As To Be Solemn and Orderly – Wang Has Ordered the Formulation of Measures to Thoroughly Improve

(Nanjing) Chairman Chiang recently inspected the uniforms and living habits of students in various schools in Nanjing and believes that they must be strictly rectified. Recently, he sent a handwritten letter to Minister of Education Wang Shijie, stating that student uniforms and hats are often untidy. He should strictly order the heads of schools to pay special attention to rectifying them. All teachers should also be responsible for inspecting and correcting them. Generally, hats must be straight and clothes must be tight to avoid developing lazy habits. Students wearing yellow uniforms should preferably wear leather belts to tighten them. He then mentioned that it is not appropriate for middle school students to have long hair and it should be banned. If principals and teachers set an example, it will be easier to rectify. It is best for principals and teachers to wear uniforms at school at all times. He also said that college students in the capital lack neatness and solemnity in their clothing and actions, and they must be ordered by the Social Affairs Bureau and the presidents of various schools to correct this. It is reported that after receiving the letter, the Minister of Education has instructed the presidents of various schools to strictly formulate measures to rectify student uniforms and promote orderly living and action, in order to ensure that they are thoroughly implemented, and will urge all schools in the country to pay attention to improvement. (6th Central News Agency Telegram)

He Yingqin Talks About the Heavy Losses Suffered by Sichuan Bandits

(Nanjing) Since the communist bandits in Sichuan Province fled north, people generally believed that the bandits led by Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, and Xu Xiangqian had all fled into Shaanxi and Gansu Provinces. It was also rumored that the bandit suppression army in northern Shaanxi was slightly disadvantaged, and that our Wang Yizhe's army had engaged in several fierce battles with the bandits, with heavy casualties on both sides. It was said that He Lizhong, the division commander, and two regimental commanders had died in battle due to serious injuries. On the 6th, the reporter specifically visited He Yingqin, Minister of Military Affairs, to inquire about the recent bandit disturbances. He replied, stating that after our army carried out a large-scale encirclement and suppression operation against the bandits led by Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, and Xu Xiangqian on the border of Sichuan and Kangding Provinces, they suffered extremely heavy losses. The forces led by Mao Zedong and Peng Dehuai, numbering about 5,000 people and about 4,000 guns, who fled into Shaanxi Province, have joined forces with a force led by Liu Zidan and Xu Haidong in Wuqizhen, Jindingshan, and other places. One force is confronting our army east of Wangjiatai. Another force led by Liu Zidan and Xu Haidong is still near Ganquan. Their main force has fled from Xiasiwan, Wangjiaping, and Longfangzhen to the front and rear Taoyuan. Last month, our Wang Yizhe's army engaged in a fierce battle with Xu Liu's main force near Ganquan. It is true that He Lizhong, the division commander of Wang's army, the chief of staff of the division, and two regimental commanders were killed in action, but the casualties of the bandits were also extremely heavy. As for the main forces led by Zhu De and Xu Xiangqian in northwestern Sichuan, they have now fled to Maogong, Fubian, Suijing, Chonghua, Danba, and other areas. One force has advanced to the east of the Lilong Pass, and another force has attacked Dapaoshan, but was defeated by our unit and fled back to Maoniu. One force has fled to Jinjun, Baoxing, and other places. However, the bandit army is running around in exhaustion, coupled with the lack of materials and manpower, and many people have fallen ill and died along the way due to hunger and cold. Our army's bunkers are tightly layered and layered, and the time for encirclement and annihilation is not far away. (6th Central News Agency Telegram)

Ji Mi District Commissioner's Office Holds Winter Defense Conference

(Beiping) The Ji Mi District Winter Defense Conference was held today at the Commissioner's Office in Tongzhou. The county magistrates of the district, including He Xiaoyi and Cao Zhen, the director of the Gubeikou Office, Huo Shi, the commander of the First Corps of the Security Team, Zhang Qingyu, and the commander of the Fifth Corps, Li Yunsheng, attended. Yin Rugeng went to Tongzhou this morning to preside over everything. The main agenda was to discuss the joint winter defense of the counties and the reorganization of county tax revenue and civil groups. (6th Special Telegram)

(Tianjin) Yin Rugeng went to Beiping on the 5th and then went to Tong County to convene the Ji Mi District Winter Defense Conference. (5th Special Telegram)

Bandits Found Disturbing the Border Between Hebei and Henan

(Tianjin) A large group of more than 500 bandits was found in Jingdianji, on the border between Hebei and Henan, on the 4th. They occupied dozens of villages and set up a puppet command headquarters. Villagers fled to Zhangde and Daming. The 119th Division sent a mortar company to suppress them and sent a letter to Henan Province to send troops to block them. (6th Special Telegram)

(Tianjin) The notorious bandit Liu Zinan gathered more than 200 bandits in Caocheng, Shandong Province, and fled to Jin Tan Town, Laoshanlou, Daming. The momentum is great. On the 4th, they launched a night attack on the county seat of Daming. The town's militia was outnumbered and forced to withdraw. The bandits entered the town and looted everything, taking more than a hundred men and women hostages, including several teachers and students from the county normal school. Sun Dequan's division has sent a battalion of troops to pursue them. It is reported that the bandits are quite organized and are still being incited by Shi Yousan. (6th Special Telegram)

Jinghui Electric Report from Shandong: Expediting the Plugging of the Dongzhuang Breach; Funding of 670,000 Yuan Already Remitted

(Nanjing) The Dongzhuang breach plugging project requires an estimated 2,670,000+ yuan in funding. The Economic Commission has decided to bear the entire cost and has telegraphed the Shandong Provincial Government, urging them to expedite the plugging construction. It is projected that the breach will be closed by April of next year and completed by June. 670,000 yuan of construction funds have already been remitted, with the remaining funds being planned for subsequent allocation. (6th Dispatch)

(Jinan) If another 1,200,000 yuan is not received before the end of the year for the breach plugging project, then the straw and stone materials will not be delivered in 80% quantity, which will inevitably delay the closing of the breach before the peach blossom flood. Zhang Honglie is determined to fight for it even at the cost of his position. Due to disaster relief efforts, the province needs 300,000 yuan per month, and all resources have been exhausted, making it impossible to take on additional burdens. Han has entrusted Kong Xiangrong to speak favorably on their behalf to the Central Government, urging the prompt allocation of construction funds. Kong is leaving for Beijing tonight, and the construction of the large materials transportation railway will be temporarily postponed. (6th Dispatch)

The Significance of the Italy-Abyssinia War in Terms of Racial Relations

— Enlin

Italy has disregarded everything and launched an attack on Abyssinia. Abyssinia is also resisting with all its national strength. Of course, this is not just a battle of wits between Black Shirt leader Mussolini and Emperor Haile Selassie. This war also encompasses significance in terms of racial and economic relations. The Black scholar W.E.B. Du Bois has written a paper on this racial relationship. The main points can be divided into two: (1) Why Italy is so determined to seize Abyssinia. (2) What lessons can colored people all over the world learn from this event? The original text is roughly as follows: (1)

In the Middle Ages, there was no real so-called race problem. Research and discussion about humanity were limited to nationality, culture, and religion. Later, a portion of the prolific ethnic groups sought to develop outwards and needed a group of laborers to serve as tools for their colonial expansion. Thus, the slave trade became a specialized industry. The practice of slave trading became prevalent everywhere, and in the New World of the Americas, various obstacles were encountered. First, people with upright ideas strongly opposed the slave system; second, the development of the democratic movement raised the status of workers. On the surface, the slave trade and slave transport seemed to have come to an end there, but in reality, this was just a trick of the white people, a mere change of the soup without changing the ingredients. As for the European imperialist countries, they turned their African territories into large warehouses, where many slaves were transshipped. By the nineteenth century, white people changed their methods and took wool from the sheep themselves, simply transplanting large numbers of African blacks to develop the African mainland. Under such circumstances, if the cultural and intellectual levels of Europeans and their subject peoples were not far apart, then the race problem would not have arisen. However, in the minds of Europeans, there were differences in status among races, and territorial expansion was necessary and justifiable; and in fact, this gave them enormous profits, making it difficult for everyone to stop. Germany, Belgium, and Italy, seeing that other countries had obtained colonial territories and reaped many benefits, naturally became envious and tried to find ways to enhance their prestige. They indeed felt early on that if they wanted to embark on the path of modern industrialism, they had to do so, or they would face death.

Asia, South America, and Africa were all open to European expansion, but the methods of expansion varied subtly. Asia is the source of culture and can be considered a family of officials and nobles, not allowing European powers to directly dominate through political force. They had to use investment as a precursor to economic invasion. However, before the Great War, Japan was able to escape European domination on its own. South America, sheltered by the Monroe Doctrine, did not suffer interference from European political forces, but the ruling white class there was served by the Indians. Although racial distinctions were not as deeply entrenched as in Asia and Africa, they were still clearly defined. As for Africa and the West Indies, white people only controlled the indigenous laborers, paying them meager wages, and there were no political facilities, education, or industrial training opportunities for them. In short, the goal was to extract the fattest profits from this laboring class.

In addition to engaging in economic development, European people insisted on racial concepts and used the guise of Christianity among the subject natives to carry out their own ulterior motives. This two-pronged approach became a bizarre phenomenon in modern times. For example, Christianity did make some contributions to the cultural construction of Africans and blacks in South America, and it also had some influence on Asia. However, in terms of industrial and economic development, it undoubtedly continuously used Christianity as a smokescreen to make the natives obedient and without revolutionary ambitions. Sometimes the missionaries were used, but they never understood what role they were playing in the play.

(2)

What has been said above mostly refers to the situation before the Great War. After the war, the racial relations of the world underwent a dramatic change, which can be said to be a revolution in racial thought. In addition to escaping the domination of Europeans, Japan emerged as a new force among the world's powers. From then on, white people could no longer arbitrarily rule the world, but had to contend with the colored races who were gradually rising and embarking on the path to freedom. For example, China is currently progressing towards her new order, and once she shakes off the current birth pangs, she will break away from the domination of white people and become an autonomous country, which everyone acknowledges. In addition, countries such as India, Haiti, and Liberia are also gradually breaking free from Eastern bonds and will soon regain their original appearance.

Abyssinia has always been subjected to relatively light restrictions, and its political autonomy has been considerable. It has also begun to change its old policies. In all respects, this black race, which has not been tainted by modern developmentists and racial prejudice, has a promising future. Unfortunately, this beautiful dream was shattered by Italy under the rule of the iron-fisted prime minister. Because she is not an industrial country and still maintains a slave system, Italy regards Abyssinia as an uncivilized barbarian. It should be known that the slave system existing in Abyssinia is completely different from slave trading and the development of territories in modern industrialism. Italy openly advocates depriving these Africans of their land, which is often the first step in cutting off their economic and political support. In fact, Italy's move is imitating its predecessors, England and France.

These countries first established economic power in Africa, and the opening shot was this method. However, in most cases, it was cleverly concealed under the guise of legality. Like Italy, which is now brazenly shouting: For the sake of our tenant farmers, we want the land of Abyssinia, which is truly rare!

There is little doubt that the main reason for the Great War was that several countries wanted to gain a foothold in the development of African territories, and here, another spark was buried. Before the war, Germany had its economic foothold in Asia and Asia Minor, and its future was very promising. However, she was not satisfied with Africa; she regretted the loss of Uganda, because the equal opportunity to develop the upper Nile basin was lost, and she undoubtedly would sooner or later advocate that Belgium abandon the Congo, and was unwilling to allow France to exclusively occupy Lake Chad and the upper Niger basin. Her desire to accomplish these claims was one of the main reasons she welcomed war.

Now everyone seems to be replaying the old tunes. Germany is determined to restore its colonies, and Italy is determined to have Britain and France fulfill the promises given to Italy in the 1915 Treaty of London. Because of this, Germany and Italy were like-minded, and Mussolini and Hitler were as close as glue, twisting together. However, good times do not last, and a sudden change occurred in the middle, because the Germans' attempt to occupy Austria inadvertently broke these plans. The Germans' move startled France and Italy, and they could not help but join hands and become friends. As a result, France no longer opposed Italy's development of East Africa. However, if Italy cuts off a pound of meat from someone by force, who can guarantee that Germany will not reproduce the original version? There are other concerns! The Arabs massacred the Armenians on a large scale because Italy seized Tripoli and Cyrenaica, and they hate them to the bone. Japan's trade volume in the Abyssinian market is not small, and Indians are ubiquitous in East African business. White developers in Africa have always forbidden them from getting involved, but now these Eastern forces have infiltrated, causing a dramatic change in issues such as political sovereignty and people's freedom.

(3)

If Italy, on the one hand, does not hesitate to spend a lot of money and use a large amount of armaments to attack Abyssinia, and on the other hand, still maintains courtesy among European countries, then Italy's victory over Abyssinia may be possible. If this is the case, the price paid by Italy and the white people for this victory will be very high. All colored races—China, India, Japan, Africa, and Africans in America—who have felt oppression and insults, and who have been enslaved and invaded by white people—should think in their hearts: "I told you so! They are untrustworthy, even among their companions. They do not believe in the principles of Christ, and they will never automatically recognize the essential elements of humanity or give up their desire to rule the majority for their own self-interest. Freedom and equality can only be achieved through strength, through great strength."

Let us now ignore the terrible scenes of bloodshed. If we expect that Abyssinia can resist the Italian invasion or remain undefeated after several months, this imagination seems difficult at present, but it is possible. Then what will be the result? The black countries will cheer with eerie music: "The shackles of the Europeans have been broken, this is the beginning of the end, and white people can no longer rely on their violence to make yellow, black, and brown people their slaves." This view is close to fantasy and is too excessive, and the contributions of Europeans and white people to the education of the spiritually-sensitive cannot be dismissed. However, this understanding is unavoidable.

Whether Italy wins or loses this war, it has already pushed the world to a fork in the road, and the envy among races will be even more profound. If Italy loses the war, the prestige of the white world will suffer a serious blow, just like Russia was defeated by Japan.

Now, among the colored races around the world, except for Japan, which is the pride of the race, the others, such as black and brown people, are gradually becoming aware and rising up. The Japanese have also imitated the ways of European white people, using military power and commercial economic power to expand outwards. At this time, Italy, disregarding everything, gives people a terrible impression. Although she is the center of Catholicism and the home of modern cultural and artistic revival, she frankly says: We want to conquer an inferior nation, not for their sake, but for our own benefit. We are going to take Abyssinia, just like we took Somaliland and Britain took Nyasaland. We want to turn black people into landless slaves. Because we have the power to do this, and no white country dares to, and no colored country can, stop us. Therefore, from the black people's point of view, under this argument, if colored countries want to maintain themselves, it is useless to hope for anything from white Europe or to appeal to religion and culture. The only way out is strength. Small and weak countries and colored races around the world can only endure and wait for the outcome of the Italy-Abyssinia dispute. Why can't the world, or any part of the world, stop this great disturbance? What we can understand is that the actions of the other countries are no different from Italy's!

Page 8

The Bank of China Reorganized into a Reserve Bank; Extreme Support from All Quarters

Reorganization Procedures Can Be Easily Realized in a Short Time; Deliberate Inclusion of Private Shares; Oversight of Government Measures

(Nanjing) Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi declared that the reorganization of the Central Bank into a Central Reserve Bank, to become a detached organization able to fully maintain the stability of the national currency, has been met with extreme support from all quarters. According to Kong, the existing Central Bank is already, in practice, acting as a bank among banks. Reorganization into the Central Reserve Bank is an easy process and can be achieved in the shortest time possible. To ensure that the people understand the actual reserve situation of the legal tender, Kong also plans to sell a proportion of the Central Reserve Bank's shares to the people, so that they can be elected as directors and supervisors of the bank in their capacity as shareholders, allowing them to oversee the government's measures regarding the new monetary policy. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) A well-known monetary economist stated that, according to Song Ziwen's assurances, the reserve amount for banknotes currently circulating on the market already exceeds 10% of the amount issued. In other words, every 100 yuan banknote has 110 yuan in reserve, an unprecedentedly ample reserve. The Chinese people have always trusted the banknotes of the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. Now that they have been reorganized into legal tender and have ample reserves, trust should be even more solid than before, and the success of the new monetary policy can be predicted. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Finance Minister Kong today told Reuters reporters his confidence that China's new currency system is bound to succeed. It is said that this new approach stabilizes the currency, restores credit, revives trade, and reverses the recession. Stability of the currency is essential. Now, the Finance Ministry's struggle against monetary instability has achieved a great victory. Reports from all over the country have indicated that the public understands and supports the Finance Ministry's policies. Friendly nations and their banks are also giving close cooperation, for which we are deeply grateful, and hope that they will continue to cooperate with the Chinese people to usher in a new era beneficial to industry and commerce, so that the Chinese and foreign people can all benefit from it. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Uniform Implementation of the New Currency System in Various Regions

Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance Also Issues Announcement of Compliance, Along with Six Measures

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance issued an announcement on the 6th to comply with the Ministry of Finance's new monetary laws, laying down six measures: 1. From November 7th onwards, all public and private receipts and payments shall be limited to legal tender. Cash may not be used, nor may it be privately hoarded. 2. The management and issuance of legal tender reserves shall be handled by a management committee jointly formed by the government and the people. 3. From the 7th, people shall exchange their existing silver for silver yuan notes at the government custodial association, with an added value of 2 jiao for small silver coins and 4 jiao for large silver coins. 4. All silver shall be sold to the provincial bank from the 7th onwards and may not be privately hoarded. 5. Contracts previously made in silver coins shall be settled in legal tender uniformly. 6. People may freely buy and sell foreign currencies they originally possess, but they may not be directly used. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Beiping city government has been ordered to use legal tender to redeem silver and banknotes from various commercial banks, so that legal tender is used uniformly on the market. After the banking association decided on the steps, each bank has separately compiled a clear statistic of its silver reserves and the amount of banknotes issued, which has been reported to the association. The association believes that the existing legal tender, Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, in Beiping city are not sufficient for its own use. Therefore, the association telegraphed Shanghai requesting a large batch of legal tender to be sent to Beiping quickly, so that the second step of the redemption work can be carried out. It is also heard that after the collection of all silver in the city, it is planned to transport it to the Central Government for preservation, so Beiping does not plan to set up a separate custodial institution. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Banking Association and the Money Trade Association held another joint meeting on the afternoon of the 5th to discuss the investigation of the amount of silver reserves in various banks in the city and requested the Ministry of Finance to establish a custodial association in Tianjin. The Ministry of Finance sent a telegram to Tianjin on the 5th, inquiring about the amount of silver reserves in Tianjin and urging a prompt report. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Banking and Money Trade Associations decided to seal up 7.8 million yuan of silver in various banks in Tianjin and plan to telegraph the Ministry of Finance requesting a temporary suspension of shipment to Shanghai as a reserve for the future Tianjin Custodial Committee. On the 6th, various commodity prices fell slightly, and the market situation was more stable. Merchants and the public believe that the Central Government's unified legal tender system is a perfect method and are enthusiastically promoting it. (6th Dispatch)

(Hankou) Since receiving the notice from the Central Bank's Hankou branch, banks in Hankou have reported in detail the amount of silver in stock and the number of banknotes issued as of November 3rd from the 6th. Foreign banks in Hankou, such as Citibank and HSBC, are able to implement the measures stipulated by the Central Government. It is heard that the number of hard coins in Hankou is about 10 million yuan. The Central Bank's Hankou branch has received several million yuan in legal tender from the head office on the 6th, which can be exchanged as much as possible at any time. For deposits in various Nanye banks, legal tender will be provided to assist in case of withdrawals and crowding. Although some foreign firms have taken a wait-and-see attitude in purchasing goods in recent days, this pause will only last for a few days. The rise in commodity prices on the market and the lack of copper coins are due to merchants and the public not understanding the situation. It is expected that it will not be difficult to calm down within a few days. The market in various places in the province, such as Yichang and Shashi, is also extremely stable. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Hankou) The Central Bank's Hankou branch notified various banks on the 5th to investigate and report the types and amounts of banknotes in stock and the amount of cash. Foreign Citibank and HSBC also changed to legal tender. However, it is difficult for unscrupulous merchants to exchange copper coins for small-scale trade, and suppression is being planned. (5th Dispatch)

(Hankou) After the improvement of the currency system, the Wuhan market is still stable, but commodity prices are soaring. The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau has strictly ordered the crackdown on hoarding and speculation and has convened the chairman of the Wuyang Chamber of Commerce to discuss stabilizing commodity prices in order to maintain finance. The Hankou authorities will also take strict measures. (6th Dispatch)

(Qingdao) Since the Ministry of Finance issued the order to reform the currency system, the price of silver dollars in the city has skyrocketed. Every 100 yuan can be exchanged for 140 to 150 yuan of paper currency. Petty merchants are secretly buying them, and the prices of various commodities have also skyrocketed. (6th Dispatch)

(Anqing) The county chamber of commerce convened a joint meeting of various industries at 4:00 PM on the 6th to discuss the implementation of a unified currency system. Director of the Department of Civil Affairs Ma Lingfu attended the meeting to provide instructions. After deliberation, it was decided that from now on, all industries will use legal tender uniformly. (6th Dispatch)

(Kaifeng) The value of the currency has fallen in reality. Every yuan has fallen from 8,200 to 7,600. The Provincial Government convened the managers of the Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications at 9:00 AM on the 6th. Qian Zonghao of the Central Bank convened various banks and money shops at 7:00 PM. The Department of Finance convened representatives of silver shops and various industries at 3:00 PM to discuss the promotion of legal tender. (6th Dispatch)

(Jinan) Today, the Central Bank convened a meeting of all banks and money houses in the city at the Banking Association, reported on the currency reform order, and ordered each bank to report the number of silver and banknote reserves held by itself and on behalf of others as of the 3rd of this month to the bank tonight in order to report it to the head office. The city's silver reserves are about 7 million yuan. Since the Department of Finance prohibited all banks from exchanging cash two months ago, the market is not affected. However, commodity prices are soaring, and finance is still tight. The Chamber of Commerce is scheduled to go to the Department of Finance on the 7th to request that the banks handle mortgage loans to activate the market, because local products are now on the market. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The Provincial Government has issued a circular to all counties stating that all receipts and payments should be made in legal tender. The city's economy is exhausted, and there is no circulation function. Silver is still extremely tight. After the various money shops were dismantled from the Central Yumin, the transaction that had fallen into stagnation was restored. However, there are still very few deposits and withdrawals. The prices of various commodities have risen. The dockworkers' union appealed to the general labor union to suppress commodity prices in order to maintain their livelihood. (6th Dispatch)

(Hangzhou) The number of people exchanging cash for legal tender at the Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications has been quite enthusiastic in recent days, about 200,000. However, unscrupulous merchants have taken the opportunity to raise the market prices of goods. The price of rice in each stall has risen by 4 jiao uniformly from today. The city chamber of commerce has specially convened a joint meeting of various industry associations to discuss suppressing commodity prices. (6th Dispatch)

(Zhenjiang) Since the Central Government announced the legal tender decree, all merchants in Zhenjiang have complied, and the market is stable. However, the exchange industry has almost invisibly closed due to the lack of market prices. Zhao Dihua, Director of the Department of Finance, specially convened the leaders of the Zhenjiang silver and money industries at noon on the 6th to discuss the issue of copper coin exchange rates. The Department of Finance stipulated that each banknote should be exchanged for 1 jiao and 2 jiao of small silver coins and 3,000 wen of copper coins, which has been submitted to the Provincial Government for review and to the Ministry of Finance for record. Once approved, it will be announced in about seven days to reassure merchants and the public and stabilize the market and will be notified to all counties for uniform compliance. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Changsha) The Central, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications released 2 million in loans to the money industry on the 5th, using goods as collateral, in order to maintain the market. If necessary, more will be released. (6th Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Since the promulgation of the nationalization of hard coins, the price of small silver coins has skyrocketed. On this day, the auxiliary coins of the Republic of China in the second and third years, transported from Hong Kong, and the silver coins cast by the province's officials, were 1 yuan of foreign currency for every ten haos of small foreign currency. Various money shops in the city are still secretly buying and selling silver, which is mostly handed over to Taiwanese to transport to Taiwan and then to Japan, which can earn a 3 jiao profit. (6th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation (HSBC) stopped paying hard coins on the 6th and issued approximately 100,000 yuan in new one-yuan banknotes. It is widely rumored in financial circles that the Hong Kong government will take the same steps as our government to implement currency management policies. Speculators are extremely active and are buying silver, causing the discount on every thousand silver dollars to be 90 yuan. The exchange rate of the Hong Kong dollar was one shilling and six and a half pence when the Agricultural Bank opened today, a decrease of half a pence compared to the 5th. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Guangzhou) The Guangdong government officially endorsed the Central Government's currency reform measures today and issued a circular tonight, prohibiting the use of silver as currency from tomorrow. The current silver situation requires the government to adopt a plan for currency control. Therefore, in addition to prohibiting the use of silver as currency, the people are not allowed to hoard silver dollars or large silver bars. Violators will be punished according to law. It is also stated that the government will never adopt a currency inflation method, and the issuance of national currency will be supervised by a preparatory committee jointly organized by the people and the government. The circular does not mention the stability measures for the exchange of Guangdong currency with foreign currencies, but the circular allows the public to continue to buy and sell Hong Kong dollars in order to facilitate foreign exchange, but Hong Kong dollars must not be directly circulated in domestic transactions. In the past two days, the price of Hong Kong dollars has skyrocketed, as the public believes that the government will eventually endorse the Central Government's currency reform measures. The premium on Hong Kong dollars reached a record high of 5 jiao 2 fen 2 today. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Peking City Government Strictly Prohibits Price Gouging and Orders Military Police to Protect All Banks

(Nanjing) The Peking City Government received a telegram from Chairman Chiang stating that the Ministry of Finance has announced that the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications will manage currency circulation with legal tender. This concerns the rectification of the currency system, the activation of finance, the relief of industry and commerce, and the stabilization of public sentiment. It is imperative to assist in the implementation of this measure to ensure its widespread adoption. However, at the beginning of the announcement, there is deep concern that the general public may not understand the true situation, leading to misunderstandings, which would allow unscrupulous elements to take the opportunity to spread rumors and disrupt public order. It is requested that subordinates be instructed to protect banks in all localities and to carefully explain the situation to the public so that they understand the truth. The City Government has replied that, as Peking is the capital of the country, all eyes are on it, and price gouging must be stopped to ensure stability. It has already sent letters to the military police, party headquarters, chambers of commerce, and guilds of money dealers to discuss methods of prevention. At the same time, in conjunction with the military police agencies, it issued a public notice. In addition to sending letters to the military police agencies to protect the banks properly, it also instructed subordinates to pay attention to the soaring prices of commodities in the market at all times and to find ways to stop it. (6th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The price of rice in Peking has stabilized, but copper coins and silver dimes have risen slightly again.
