Mayor of Peiping, Yuan Liang, Approved to Resign

—Vacancy Temporarily Filled by Song Zheyuan—

Peiping Correspondence: Yuan Liang, the mayor of Peiping, has been in office here and has made considerable achievements in local construction. The most notable of these is that most of the main roads in the city have been paved with asphalt. The reorganization of cultural relics of the old capital has also been effective. As for the supervision of water and electricity utilities, both companies have been able to comply with orders. In the field of education, he trained and selected teachers and increased the number of schools. Unexpectedly, a bolt from the blue struck, and he was subject to extraordinary constraints. Therefore, on November 1, he submitted a request to the Central Government to resign from his post. On the 3rd, he received a reply from the Executive Yuan approving his request. Yuan immediately summoned the principals of various schools that evening to say goodbye. They were silent and speechless. Yuan said with emotion that the responsibility of those who run education is greater than those who run politics, and the methods of those who run politics are more difficult than those who run education. Therefore, I hope that you will continue to work hard in education with the spirit of enjoying it. As for my running politics, looking back, I cannot say that I have no perseverance, but I still cannot break through or resist the difficulties. How painful it is! Many of those present wept when they heard this. Finally, they said goodbye to each other. On the 4th, Yuan had already left Peiping by car to go south.

The Peiping Municipal Government's administrative plan for the 24th year is to complete the first step of the construction of the scenic area. As of now, one-third of the first step has been completed. Yuan's plan was to make visitors enjoy themselves so much that they would forget to return, and to thoroughly understand the long history of Chinese culture and its great spirit. He never expected that this plan would encounter unexpected setbacks just as it was beginning. The unfinished work will rely on the successor to complete. Song Zheyuan, who was ordered to temporarily take over as mayor, took office on the morning of the 5th. In his speech to the staff after taking office, Song also said that he would like to continue to work on Yuan's plan and declared that he hoped that you would continue to work hard with the spirit of service you had when Mayor Yuan was in office. Therefore, it is expected that Yuan's unfinished work will not be interrupted. However, Chen Baoshu, the secretary-general of the Municipal Government, and others resigned and have been approved by Yuan before his departure. Cai Yuan, the director of the Social Affairs Bureau, and others also requested to resign to Song in person, and Song earnestly tried to persuade them to stay. (5th)

More Than 50 Organizations in Guangzhou Welcome Hu Wenhu

2,000 People from All Walks of Life Arrived at the Station to Welcome Him

Commanders Chen and Li Both Hosted Banquets to Welcome Him

Hu Wenhu, a member of the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee and a leader in sports among overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia, personally led the Malaysian Chinese athletes to attend the National Games and was warmly welcomed by people from all over the country. On the 1st, he arrived in Hong Kong by boat. Hu took the opportunity to return to the country and made a special trip to Guangdong to visit and inspect the construction of the province. When the local authorities here heard the news, they sent representatives to Hong Kong to welcome Hu. Yesterday (the 1st) afternoon, Hu, along with the welcoming representatives and accompanying secretaries Ye Guisong, You Fanwu, and Hu Cimei, arrived in the province on the Guangzhou-Kowloon Express. The details of their arrival in the port are recorded below:

Arrival at Port

The express train that Hu was on departed from Hong Kong at 8:00 a.m. and arrived at the Da Shatou Station at 11:25 a.m. In advance, a platoon of 15 military police was dispatched, and the Qianjian Branch dispatched police officers to protect the station. The people who arrived at the station to welcome him included Wen Taihua, representing Commander Chen, Chen Guoliang, representing Commander Li, Lin Yizhong, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Huang Linshu, Director of the Department of Education, Hu Weiwan, President of the Aviation School, Shen Yangong, representing the Fujian Fellow Villagers Association, Zeng Xiaofeng and Shao Zongmeng, Directors of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee, Hu Shuxin, representing the Provincial and Municipal Chambers of Commerce and the Guangdong Provincial Hu Clan Association, representatives from the Guangdong Renai Benevolent Hall, the Sacred Spirit Orphanage, the Holy Infant Nursery, the Jianzhong Middle School, the Huadi Orphanage, the National University, Lingnan University, and various overseas Chinese charitable organizations, and about 2,000 people from all walks of life. They were all lined up on the platform of the Da Shatou Station. After the train arrived, Hu stepped out of the carriage, music played loudly, and the welcoming personnel boarded the train one after another to shake hands with Hu as a courtesy. Then, they filed out of the station, changed to cars, and toured along Baiyun Road, Changdi, Taiping Road, and Yonghan Road, and arrived at the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee on Dadong Road. There were more than 100 cars to welcome him at the station. Firecrackers were set off along the way, and the scene was extremely lively.

Welcome Reception

The Guangdong Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee held a meeting at the Provincial Council Hall on Dadong Road to welcome Hu as a giant among overseas Chinese. All the members of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee were present, as well as representatives from the Joint Office of the British and Dutch Colonies in Southeast Asia, the American Alliance Association, the China National Federation of Machine Workers, the Overseas Comrades Society, the Overseas Chinese Industrial Federation, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the General Headquarters, the Renai Benevolent Hall, the Army General Hospital, Zhongshan University, Lingnan University, and more than 50 other organizations, as well as all the boy scouts of the National University and Jianzhong Middle School, the Orphan Education Institute, and all the staff and students of the Holy Infant Nursery. During the meeting, Lin Yizhong delivered a welcoming speech, briefly inviting Mr. Hu to come to Guangdong this time. The association is holding a meeting here to welcome him and hopes that Mr. Hu will strongly support the charitable undertakings, industry, culture, and construction of this province. Then, Hu gave a reply, saying that he had two purposes for returning to the country this time: (1) to lead the Malaysian Chinese athletes to Shanghai to participate in the National Games; (2) to visit various construction projects in the motherland and inspect the industries of various provinces, in preparation for future investment. I am very honored to be invited by you today. The speakers included Wen Taihua, representing the General Headquarters, Huang Linshu, Director of the Department of Education, and representatives from the Overseas Comrades Society and the Overseas Chinese Industrial Federation of Southeast Asia, who highly praised Hu's various undertakings. At about 1:00 p.m., the meeting ended happily, and they went to the New Asia Hotel to rest. At 2:30 p.m., he attended a banquet hosted by Chairman Lin of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Committee at the Taiping Restaurant, and then went to the Hu Clan Ancestral Hall for a welcome meeting, and participated in the groundbreaking ceremony of the Hu Clan Memorial Hall. In the evening, he attended a banquet hosted by Commander Chen at Meihua Village, where they had a very pleasant conversation. The next day, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the National University held a welcome banquet. On the third day, he returned to Hong Kong by car.

Songjiang: Two Thieves Who Hid Jewelry Captured

The 14th Security Brigade, while protecting the highway the day before yesterday, discovered that one of the passengers in Minhang was hiding gunpowder, which violated the prohibition. They also found a lot of jewelry, gold, and silverware hidden in the legs of his trousers. Recognizing that he was not a good person, they detained him together with another passenger who looked flustered. They found more pieces of gold and silver jewelry. After interrogating them, they confessed that they had robbed the home of an unknown person outside the South Gate of Songjiang County and the home of Xi Genfa in Yexie. There was also a small boat moored in the Xiaonei River in Minhang. They were taken there for a search, and four more accomplices were captured. After questioning, they confessed their names: Wang Asan, Chen Ada, Zhu Aer, Xu Dezhong, Zhou Aer, and Wang Ada. After hearing the news, the County Public Security Bureau sent Detective Sun Shaoqing to Minhang with the victim Xi Genfa to identify them. The people and the stolen goods were correct. They returned to Songjiang and reported, and will send a document to Minhang to transfer them to Songjiang for trial.

Suzhou: Hongtai Money Shop Suddenly Closes

The Hongtai Money Shop in the Dongzhong Market of Banmennei, which was a Shouzih-grade shop, had been open for five years. It was jointly opened by the Xi Honggao Opera Costume Shop. The manager was Bian Rongsen from Zhenjiang, and the assistant manager was Chen Jieliang. Because the assistant manager embezzled money, they all ran away at about 4:00 a.m. on the 6th, along with more than ten employees. The manager also disappeared at the same time. Bian's family had moved to Suzhou and left Suzhou a week earlier. The shop's cash ledger and employee guarantee were also taken away. The preparations were extremely thorough in advance. After hearing the news, the Money Dealers' Guild held an emergency meeting in the afternoon. It is reported that more than 100,000 yuan was embezzled. Because the dealings with other money shops were not large, the bad debts were not large.

The Son Murder Case Proved to Be Suicide by Hanging

Zao Wang, the son of Wu Jiangshi, who lived on Guimen Street outside Banmen, suddenly died. There were rumors that he was strangled to death by his mother. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the local prosecutor's office sent personnel to conduct a detailed examination on the afternoon of the 5th. The conclusion was that he had indeed committed suicide by hanging himself. When the examination was conducted, there were one or two thousand spectators. Only after the examination was confirmed was the truth revealed.

Wuxi: Copper Coins Plunge, Shaking the Market

In Wuxi, the market price of copper coins in the past month was as high as 3,500 wen per yuan due to the large number of coins being released. At the beginning of this month, the price gradually fell back to 3,260 wen due to the gradual increase in sales. Unexpectedly, after the Ministry of Finance announced its policy of reforming the currency system, a certain yarn factory took advantage of the opportunity to purchase cotton clothes at the place of production and collected a large number of copper coins. Various tobacco shops took the opportunity to manipulate the market, causing a sudden shortage of copper coins in the market and a plunge in the exchange rate to 1,000 wen. On the morning of the 5th, the Money Dealers' Guild also stated that there was a great demand for copper coins from all parties, but very few were released, so they made an opening price, which fell to 2,700 wen. In the afternoon, the market was even more short of copper coins. The tobacco shops were manipulating the market again, and it was even impossible to exchange them anywhere. The market was extremely chaotic. The Chamber of Commerce also received long-distance telephone calls from the chambers of commerce of Wujin and Suzhou, inquiring about the market situation and reporting that the market price in Suzhou and Changzhou was still 3,050 wen per yuan. On the morning of the 6th, the Money Dealers' Guild saw that there was very little source of copper coins and that the demand was still strong, so they made an opening price, which fell sharply to 1,400 wen for purchase and 2,400 wen for sale. Within three days, the exchange rate per yuan differed by as much as 8 or 900 wen, which was unprecedented in previous years. Compared with Shanghai, Hangzhou, and the counties along the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, the difference was also significant. It was clearly a deliberate attempt to raise prices and monopolize the market. On the 6th, a special telegram was sent to the Central Government, requesting the county to investigate the matter thoroughly in order to stabilize the market and prevent disruption.

Hangzhou: Red Pill Manufacturer Executed by Firing Squad

Xu Jinshan from Jiangxi used to run a paper-making business in Shouchang County, Zhejiang Province. From 1925 to 1926, he secretly set up a red pill manufacturing plant in the county and sold them widely in Qu County, Suichang, Chun'an and other counties, accumulating huge wealth. Someone secretly reported him to the Public Security Bureau, which sent police to search and found more than a dozen bags of red pills, weighing more than 170 taels, and arrested Miao Zunzhou, the red pill manufacturing technician, and Chen Sanshou and other accomplices. Unexpectedly, the criminal was very capable and colluded with Yang Chun, a member of the county party headquarters, and Miao Maolian, a patrol officer, who actually allowed him to be released on bail. The case was referred to the province, and Xu Jinshan, Chen Sanshou, and Miao Zunzhou were sentenced to death. Wu Bingwang, Yang Chun, Miao Maolian, and others were sentenced to imprisonment. At 10:00 a.m. on the 6th, the Security Department escorted the two criminals Xu and Chen to the Zhakou execution ground and executed them by firing squad.

Yangzhou: Chief Justice of Jiangsu High Court Visits Yangzhou for Inspection

Zhu Shusheng, the Chief Justice of the Jiangsu High Court, believes that the judiciary of the counties north of the Yangtze River urgently needs to be thoroughly reformed. Although he usually receives written reports from local courts, he wants to seek reform, but he has no way to start because he doesn't know the real situation. He has visited Xuzhou and Huai'an. After completing the inspection in Huaiyin, he went south on the Qingjia wheel with Shi, a clerk from the High Court. He arrived in Yangzhou on the evening of the 4th and stayed at the Dalu Hotel on Xinsheng Street. On the morning of the 5th, he went to Yizheng County for inspection. In the afternoon, he returned to Yangzhou and then went to the Jiangdu District Court for a week of inspection. He inquired in detail about the judicial situation in the county. Then, Luo Zhikao, the president of the Jiangdu Court, Li Weishan, the chief prosecutor, and Zou Shumin, the clerk, accompanied Judge Zhu to visit the detention center. Zhu first read through the various prisoner registers, and then went to the prison to inspect separately, giving many instructions on the hygiene and reform of the prisoners.

Local News

Ministry of Finance Regulations on Legal Tender and the Real Situation of Financial Stability in Shanghai

The Issuing Reserve Committee Investigates the Reserves of Various Banks Yesterday and Designates a Treasury to Store Legal Tender Reserves. Various Countries Issue Announcements Endorsing Legal Tender.

Following the Ministry of Finance's announcement that the notes of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications are legal tender, the financial situation in Shanghai has tended towards stability. The Issuing Reserve Committee investigated the issuing reserves of various banks yesterday. The Municipal Joint Association issued an announcement endorsing the legal tender. Silver firms and money shops are setting "Hui Tou" and "Hua Tou" exchange rates. The secretly marked notes of the three banks have ceased to be reissued and are being gradually withdrawn. The Central Mint is preparing to mint subsidiary currency. The China Industrial Association held a meeting yesterday to increase production. Detailed information obtained is recorded as follows:

Legal Tender Reserves - Designated Treasury

After the establishment of the Issuing Reserve Management Committee, the rules of procedure have been drafted by Xu Kan and others and are nearing completion. After the Minister of Finance, Kong Xiangxi, returns to Shanghai, a second meeting will be held to pass them. As for the legal tender reserves, the committee has designated the treasuries of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications as reserve treasuries. However, the silver dollar ingots, etc., minted by the Central Mint, after being examined and approved, will be stored in the factory, completing the Ministry of Finance's great treasury, and will not be used as legal tender issuing reserves.

Investigating the Issuing Reserves of Various Banks

In addition to the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, whose banknotes have been announced by the Ministry of Finance as legal tender, there are still ten other banks issuing banknotes (i.e., Zhongnan), China Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Siming Bank, Commercial Bank, Reclamation Bank, Agricultural and Commercial Bank, China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, China Agricultural Cooperative Bank, and Zhejiang Local Bank. However, the head office of Zhejiang Local Bank is in Hangzhou, and the head office of China Farmers' Bank is in Hankou. Yesterday, the Issuing Reserve Management Committee sent Committee Member Ye Zhuotang to Zhejiang Industrial Bank and others to investigate the issuing reserves. It is reported that he will continue to investigate China Industrial Bank and others today.

Bank's Secretly Marked Notes Have Been Withdrawn

After the banknotes of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications were designated as legal tender, market demand increased sharply. Taking Shanghai as an example, the three banks issued approximately six million yuan in banknotes on the fourth day and approximately ten million yuan in banknotes on the fifth day. As for the secretly marked notes previously issued by the three banks to adjust the financial situation, they were issued to various money shops and banks with preferential measures. Since the fourth day, they have been gradually withdrawn and have ceased to be reissued. However, small banks and small money shops that rely on secretly marked notes as an important part of their business will be affected and will have to change their business policies.

Separate Research on "Hui Tou" and "Hua Tou" Exchange Rates

Zhu Boquan, manager of the Bank Joint Reserve Committee, and Qin Xiqing, manager of the Money Shop Joint Reserve, have conducted separate research. After drafting detailed measures, they will schedule a meeting with the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications to determine the rates. The negotiable instruments circulating in the Shanghai silver and money industry are divided into "Hui Tou" and "Hua Tou". "Hui Tou" refers to the money that money shops exchange between each other, which can be offset against each other at the "Hui Hua Zong Hui" on the same night. "Hua Tou" refers to the silver that money shops exchange with Chinese and foreign banks, which must be delivered in cash on the same day. In other words, "Hui Tou" refers to next-day transactions, while "Hua Tou" refers to same-day transactions.

Bank of China Announces Foreign Exchange Rates

The Central Bank of China announced foreign exchange rates yesterday morning: one British pound was equal to one shilling and two and a half pence, twenty-nine yuan and seventy-five cents for New York, four hundred and fifty francs for Paris, seventy-three and a half marks for Berlin, one hundred and three yuan for Japan, and seventy-nine yuan for Hong Kong. The above rates are per one hundred yuan of foreign currency, equivalent to one thousand one hundred and forty-nine yuan of Shanghai tael silver. One Customs Gold Unit is equivalent to two yuan, two jiao, seven fen, and one li of national currency, equivalent to thirty-two pence and nine three seven five of British gold, and sixty-seven cents and six two five of American gold. The Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee announced the equalization tax rate at 10:00 yesterday morning as 57.25%, a decrease of 1.25% from the previous day.

Municipal Joint Association Announces Support Yesterday

The Municipal Joint Association issued a special notice to its members yesterday in support of the currency system policy, stating: "This notice concerns the six major points of the currency policy announced by the Ministry of Finance of the National Government on the fourth of this month. Its main purpose is to seek financial stability and achieve the revival of the national economy, enriching the country and benefiting the people. It is truly admirable. All measures are well-considered. All citizens, for the sake of the country and for their own sake, should express their support and jointly enter the path of prosperity. Therefore, we hereby notify all members to widely publicize and ensure that all citizens know the beauty and goodness of the policy, rise up together to support it, and diligently implement it. This is not only the duty of our citizens, but also a good sign for the future of the country. This is a special notice."

National Goods Industry Association's Telegram of Support

The Shanghai National Goods Factories Joint Association sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, supporting the legal tender: "To Minister Kong, Ministry of Finance, Nanjing: We have previously submitted a document requesting the abandonment of the silver standard and the reform of the currency system to prevent the outflow of silver and to relieve the plight of agriculture, industry, and commerce, and have sent representatives to Beijing to petition. We are grateful for your humble inquiries. We have long known that you are determined to implement the great plan to save the country. Now, we have received the emergency decree promulgated on November 4, stipulating that the banknotes issued by the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications are legal tender and cannot be redeemed for cash, and that violators will have their assets confiscated in full. From now on, we will use legal tender to relieve agriculture and industry, compile international exchange rates, strictly manage the issuance, and strive to realize the great plan of revival as soon as possible. Friendly nations are assisting us, and Chinese and foreigners alike admire your plans. Our association will lead all members and factories to express our sincerity and respectfully submit our sentiments. We sincerely hope that you will take note of this. Lu Xingzhuang, Chairman of the Shanghai National Goods Factories Joint Association; Zhang Zilian, Ma Jisheng, Tu Kaizheng, and other standing committee members; and all members kowtow." (Seal)

Industrial Meeting Discusses Steps

The China Industrial Association convened a temporary membership meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday to discuss financial issues. Representatives from the Meilin Company, Ya Pu Er Electric Appliance Factory, Great China Rubber Factory, Fuxin Flour Mill, Commercial Press, Dachen Yarn Factory, Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, Zhanghua Woolen Mill, Wing On Yarn Factory, China Cement Company, Renfeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, Tianchu MSG Factory, Tianli Gas Factory, and others attended. Guo Shun chaired the meeting (Qian Chengxu substituted). As a result of the discussions, the following steps that the production sector should take after the currency system reform were agreed upon in principle: (A) purchase of raw materials, (B) financial transactions, (C) contract orders, and (D) price stability. After detailed study by each member, the opinions will be submitted to the general secretary within three days to compile a catalog, which will be explained in detail and submitted to the Economic Struggle Committee for research. Representatives from the Qingdao, Jinan, Suzhou, and Changzhou branches will then convene a regular meeting to discuss implementation. The meeting then adjourned.

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Announces Strict Prohibition of Intentionally Raising Prices

Excessive Price Increases Beyond Cost Will Be Deemed as Violations of Orders. Four Measures Are Stipulated, and the Chamber of Commerce Is Instructed to Advise.

The Ministry of Finance's promulgation of legal tender this time was originally a major plan for economic recovery and financial stability. However, some unscrupulous merchants took the opportunity to manipulate and hoard goods, causing various prices to rise sharply, especially rice, which is related to the people's food. Therefore, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, under the order of the Municipal Government, issued a notice this morning stipulating four measures, and violators will be severely punished. At the same time, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce was instructed to advise. The original text is recorded as follows:

Social Affairs Bureau Notice: The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau's Notice states: "The currency policy promulgated by the Ministry of Finance this time is a crucial plan for economic recovery, financial stability, and national welfare. We have repeatedly and clearly prohibited any attempts to speculate and raise prices. However, in the past two days, prices in this city have soared, which is obviously due to the manipulation and hoarding by a small number of merchants, which is extremely illegal. In addition to instructing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to order all trade associations to submit fair price lists for review, anyone who intentionally raises prices will be dealt with according to the law. In addition to reporting and issuing separate orders, the measures for dealing with price increases are hereby announced to the public. This notice."

Stipulated Measures: Four attached measures: (1) Each trade association should, within three days, negotiate prices based on the amount of cost. If the negotiated prices exceed the cost too much and there is suspicion of intentionally raising prices, it will be deemed as resisting central government orders, and all executive committee members of the trade association will be held responsible. (2) Each trade association may notify all members to comply with the negotiated prices in advance and submit the negotiated price list and verification standards to the bureau for record at the same time. (3) Regardless of whether each trade association has industry regulations or whether the industry regulations have been approved, the negotiated price list must be compulsorily observed by all members, whether they are exclusively or concurrently operating, and whether they are members or non-members. (4) Those who violate the negotiated prices and arbitrarily lower prices may still be dealt with in accordance with the approved industry regulations.

Instructing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: The Municipal Government's instruction No. 16162 states: "The currency policy promulgated by the Ministry of Finance this time is a crucial plan for economic recovery and financial stability. We have repeatedly and clearly prohibited any attempts to speculate and raise prices. However, in the past two days, prices in this city have soared. For example, the price of rice has risen by as much as one or two yuan, which is obviously due to the manipulation and hoarding by unscrupulous merchants. If they are not severely punished, it will not be enough to deter evil and maintain local peace. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau to promptly and effectively crack down on this and arrest unscrupulous merchants who violate orders for investigation and prosecution according to the law, we hereby instruct you to earnestly comply and promptly report the compliance situation." Upon receiving this instruction, the bureau found that a small number of merchants were manipulating prices and intentionally raising them, which was extremely illegal. Therefore, the bureau instructed the chamber to comply and order all trade associations to negotiate balanced prices based on the amount of cost within three days of receiving this document, and to notify all trades to comply compulsorily, regardless of whether they are exclusively or concurrently operating, and whether they are members or non-members. The price list and verification standards should be submitted to the bureau for record. If the price list is found to exceed the cost excessively and there is suspicion of intentionally raising prices, it will be deemed as resisting central government orders and will be severely punished. All executive committee members of the trade association will be held fully responsible. Those who do not comply with the prices negotiated by the trade association and intentionally raise prices will be punished in accordance with central government orders. Those who violate the price list approved by the bureau and arbitrarily lower prices may still be dealt with in accordance with the promulgated industry regulations. In addition to reporting and announcing, you are hereby ordered to comply and report the compliance situation for record without delay. This order.

Mint to Mint Subsidiary Currency

After the Money Trade Association received instructions to regulate the price of subsidiary currency, with small silver dollars set at 1.2 jiao per legal tender yuan and copper coins set at 300 coins per legal tender yuan, the market price in the money trade market has been set at 833.3 yuan per jiao and 300,000 per copper coin. It is reported that the Central Mint will also mint nickel subsidiary currency in four denominations: 5 li, 1 jiao, 1.5 jiao, and 2.5 jiao, to facilitate circulation.

Nationalization of Silver Has Shown Practical Results

After the six measures promulgated by the Ministry of Finance stipulated that all silver should be nationalized, the Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee, in order to actively prevent the outflow of silver, has been increasing the export equalization tax rate on silver daily since the fourth day. The tax rate announced the day before yesterday was 58.5%, reaching the highest level. This morning, Xi Demao, Bei Songsun, and Zhang Peishen, members of the Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, jointly discussed and determined the equalization tax rate to be 57.25%, restoring the same tax rate as on the fourth day, which is still 50.5% higher than the 6.75% of the previous month. Judging from the situation, the nationalization of silver has shown practical results.

Mortgage of Real Estate Will Be Realized

Regarding the mortgage of real estate, in addition to stipulating that the Central Bank will be the reserve bank and will no longer engage in ordinary commercial banking business, the promulgated decree specifically allows the establishment of real estate mortgage banks to invigorate real estate and alleviate the stagnant state of the real estate economy in the past. The declining real estate industry in the city is reportedly delighted by this news and will proceed to discuss the realization of real estate mortgages. However, all parties believe that this should be handled prudently to avoid affecting the gradually stabilizing financial situation.

Unity of the Industry and Unified Market Prices

During this autumn of industrial and commercial decline, most industries are engaging in large-scale dumping due to market depression in order to sell off goods. If this continues, they will all perish. However, since the implementation of the new currency system, each industry, in order to seek the development of its own interests, deeply knows that it will not succeed without the unity of the industry and unified market prices. Therefore, in recent days, various industry associations have held meetings one after another to discuss various issues such as unified market prices and the cessation of dumping. This is truly the only good sign for the future of China's industry and commerce.

Mr. Zheng Hongnian Expresses His Opinion

During the 19th year of the Republic of China, the United States, due to the excessively low price of silver, intended to lend us 100 million ounces of silver. If we had accepted it at that time and used it as a foundation, and further contracted with silver-producing countries to purchase it, making China the world's silver market, the financial panic in the past two years would not have occurred. In October of last year, the government ordered the collection of silver export tax and equalization tax, but the remedy for the outflow was very small. Now, the financial authorities have resolutely implemented a unified currency system policy to prevent the outflow of silver. This is the only pivot for the economic recovery of our country. This move is most suitable for the current situation in our country, but the implementation method must realistically take into account all aspects. According to my personal opinion: (1) The government should realistically make it clear to the national populace that this policy is not currency inflation. Most importantly, it must be made clear to the remote villages and hamlets. This must be the responsibility of the village chiefs of each district to explain it. Although the people do not have large amounts of silver to hoard, some of them certainly do. Therefore, it must be explained to avoid future disturbances by unscrupulous elements under this pretext. (2) I agree with the participation of financial leaders in the organization of the Reserve Management Committee, but financial leaders sometimes cannot but focus on their own interests. Therefore, other leaders from all walks of life must participate at the same time, such as leaders from free professions such as lawyers, accountants, economic experts, and the education sector. Also, reserve sub-treasuries should be established in various places where banks are located, so that the public can know about them nearby, and leaders of this kind must also participate. In addition, there are two other points: (A) A review committee must be organized, and the selection of personnel should be as above. They must conduct a strict review once a week and make it public. This is because the level of the Chinese people is uneven, and the method of credit investigation must be particularly truthful. (B) In addition to cash and securities, real estate can also be included in the reserve treasury, but a uniform composition must be stipulated. I believe that real estate prices will definitely rise to avoid future impact. (3) Controlling international trade, it is very right for the government to unconditionally purchase and sell foreign exchange in order to stabilize the exchange rate of the national currency, but merchants often inevitably take this opportunity to speculate. The government should also control international trade at the same time, and the government should purchase needed goods in bulk and sell them to merchants. (4) Controlling copper coins, the living standard of the Chinese people is too low (there are still people living on more than one yuan per month). Copper coins cannot be abolished, but there should be a realistic statistic on the demand for copper coins in various places, and we must pray that the supply and demand correspond. The government should stipulate a legal price and hand it over to silver and money shops in various places for circulation, and hoarding is not allowed. Because China is currently short of copper, a panic will definitely occur if it is allowed to be hoarded. This level must be considered first. I remember that in the 32nd year before the founding of the Republic of China, a great panic occurred in Ning'e due to the shortage of copper coins. Later, casting was rushed, and the price of copper soared, causing the treasury to suffer a great loss. In recent times, situations that have occurred in the world and in our own country, and historical precedents near and far in our country, can be examined in considerable detail. Therefore, it is impossible not to prevent this in advance. Various economic experts have issued very good opinions, and I will not talk about it anymore. I only hope that the whole country will study appropriate methods in practice and work together with one heart and one mind with the government to save the economic crisis.

Overseas Chinese in Dutch East Indies Seek National Goods for Exhibition in Southeast Asia

Special Request for Consul-General Song to Come to Shanghai for Negotiations and Letter to National Products Manufacturers Association for Assistance

The Shiye News Agency reports that the United Federation of Chinese Chambers of Commerce in the Dutch East Indies, the General Association of Overseas Chinese Importers, and the Batavia Chinese Chamber of Commerce have jointly launched the "National Products Touring Exhibition in Southeast Asia" to promote trade in Southeast Asia and provide overseas Chinese in various places with the opportunity to gain a deep understanding of national goods. It is scheduled to be held in April next year. In addition to inviting Consul-General Song to come to Shanghai for negotiations, these organizations have also sent a letter to the Shanghai National Products Manufacturers Association for assistance. The original letter is recorded below:

Consul Song's Letter: (Beginnings Omitted) I, Faxiang, am attending the Fifth National Congress and arrived in Shanghai on the 3rd of this month. I will enter Beijing tomorrow night. I plan to meet with your association during my stay in Shanghai to discuss the preparations for the National Goods Exhibition and report on the restrictions on imports by the Dutch East Indies authorities to seek advice. I respectfully request that you discuss this matter with the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China in advance and designate a time and place for a meeting for this purpose. To the China National Products Manufacturers Association, Song Faxiang.

Letter from Overseas Chinese Merchants: It has been investigated that this port originally intended to invite representatives of domestic manufacturers who participated in the Singapore National Goods Exhibition of British Malaya to bring samples to Batavia for display. However, the representatives of the manufacturers were unable to complete the preparations in time due to the short time, and the progress was reported to the Ministry of Industry by our Consul-General Song stationed in Batavia for inspection. Now, we have received a notice from Consul-General Song, a letter from Mr. Wang Zhisheng, the chief representative of the Shanghai National Goods Manufacturers Delegation, stating that it has been decided to prepare for the National Goods Touring Exhibition in Southeast Asia in 1925, to be held in April next year. Taking advantage of the night markets held in various regions of the Dutch East Indies, the exhibition will tour Batavia, Bandung, Semarang, and Surabaya. This move is extremely important for the promotion of national goods and should be a priority for us to strive to prepare. It has been investigated that the largest-scale night markets held in the Dutch East Indies are the Gambir Night Market in Batavia, which is held from the end of August to the beginning of September each year, for about 10 or 14 days. All special products or manufactured goods from various islands of the Dutch East Indies are transported to the night market for exhibition and promotion. Hundreds of thousands of people from various ports and provinces come to visit. In recent years, an Annam Pavilion has been set up in the night market to exhibit and promote Annam's products. The pavilion is organized by the French Annam government, and all liaison matters here are presided over by the French Consul-General stationed in Batavia. Since the exhibitions over the years, it has given people here a very good impression of the local products. For the sake of promoting national goods in Southeast Asia, we should imitate the Annam method. Our association has held meetings to discuss and decided to set up a Chinese Pavilion to participate in the night market to be held in August next year, expand publicity, and facilitate promotion. Since many people from various ports come to Batavia to visit the Gambir Night Market, it seems unnecessary to expand the exhibition in Surabaya, Semarang, and Bandung to save costs. The cost of establishing the Chinese Pavilion is estimated to be about 3,000 guilders for construction and lighting. We plan to collect several types of goods for the Chinese Pavilion this time and display them in several rooms, which will require a certain amount of land. All of this should be prepared accurately, and the required expenses will inevitably be considerable. It is necessary to request a subsidy from the central government. All issues concerning the entry tax to be paid by each manufacturer's representative coming to Batavia for the exhibition and the permission for the entry of goods can be said to be the responsibility of Consul-General Song, who will liaise with the Immigration Bureau and the Ministry of Economy of the Dutch East Indies government. The round-trip tickets for the representatives coming to Batavia and Shanghai can also be handled by Consul-General Song, who will liaise with the Java Steamship Company and request a half-price discount. The Batavia Chinese Chamber of Commerce can raise 2,000 to 3,000 guilders to subsidize the expenses of this exhibition. In addition to submitting a report to the Ministry of Industry for inspection and approval for a subsidy, our association has specifically invited Consul-General Song to be the plenipotentiary representative to be responsible for liaising with the Ministry of Industry, the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the China National Products Manufacturers Association, and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to prepare for this matter. In addition to sending separate letters, this letter is sent to your association for your information. We hope that you will provide assistance when Consul-General Song visits your association to facilitate the progress. To the China Manufacturers Association, Jian Fuhui, Chairman of the United Federation of Chinese Chambers of Commerce in the Dutch East Indies; Liang Bingnong, General Affairs; Zhuang Xiyan, Chairman of the General Association of Overseas Chinese Importers; Lin Qiansun, General Affairs; Guo Tianru, Chairman of the Batavia Chinese Chamber of Commerce; Wu Weikang, General Director.

Pledge Loan for Telegraph Administration Bonds Totaling Six Million Yuan

Draft Contract Agreed Upon, to be Taken to Beijing for Report, Solely for the Development of Telegraph Administration

After the Ministry of Communications issued ten million yuan of Telegraph Administration Bonds, the Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau, led by Director Shen Shuyu, negotiated a pledge with the Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Communications Bank, which was successful. The total amount was determined to be six million yuan. The contract has been negotiated and will be signed soon. The details are as follows:

Total Amount Determined: Six Million Yuan

After negotiations between Shen Shuyu, Director of the Postal Remittances and Savings Bureau, Zhou Shouliang, Deputy Director, Zhou Youduan, Section Chief of the Ministry of Communications, and various banks, the total amount of the Telegraph Administration Bond pledge loan has now been determined. Bonds with a face value of ten million yuan will be pledged for six million yuan in cash at a 60% discount. The loan contract has been drafted and has been negotiated with the borrowing banks by Section Chief Zhou Youduan in recent days. Agreements have been reached on interest rates and terms. Only textual revisions remain.

Bank of China and Other Banks Separately Acknowledge Borrowing

The borrowing banks are the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Communications Bank, the Shanghai Bank, the Jin City Bank, the Continental Bank, the Yanyeh Bank, the Zhongnan Bank, the Kenye Bank, the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, the China National Goods Bank, and the Guohua Bank. The allocated amounts have been determined, ranging from ten thousand yuan to one million yuan. The Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Communications Bank account for the majority. Except for the Central Bank, the other banks, such as the Bank of China and the Communications Bank, have decided to organize a syndicate to handle it. In the future, when the contract is signed, the Central Bank will sign a separate contract, while the others will sign a general contract.

After Draft Contract is Signed, Return to Beijing Immediately

Zhou Youduan, Section Chief of the Ministry of Communications, has decided that after the draft pledge loan contract is negotiated, he will first sign the draft contract, and then Section Chief Zhou will take the contract back to Beijing to report to Minister Zhu Jiahua. After the Ministry of Communications approves it, it will be formally signed. This loan is entirely for the development of the telegraph administration. It has been decided to first print pre-subscription coupons and then exchange them after the official bonds are printed.

Economic Doctorate Cheng Shaode's Opinion on the Currency Reform Bill

Major Success Achieved After Long-term Implementation in European and American Countries, Fluctuations in Foreign Exchange and Commodity Prices Arise Without Impact

In order to stabilize finance, the Ministry of Finance officially telegraphed the implementation of the new currency system the day before yesterday. This matter has aroused significant attention both domestically and abroad. However, various circles may not yet fully understand the implementation of this new currency system. The Xin Shi News Agency reporter specially visited Dr. Cheng Shaode, an economist, yesterday, and he agreed to express his opinion on the currency reform bill in detail. The following is a special record:

The government announced six articles of currency reform on November 3. The main points are: first, the banknotes of the Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Communications Bank shall be legal tender; second, the banknotes of other issuing banks shall continue to be used, but only to the total amount circulating as of November 3, and no additional issuance shall be allowed. The Ministry of Finance shall determine a deadline and gradually exchange them for Central Bank banknotes; third, establish a management committee for the issuance reserve, and centralize the custody of silver reserves; fourth, from November 4, silver coins are not allowed to circulate and should be immediately exchanged for legal tender; fifth, contracts denominated in silver coins shall be settled in legal tender; sixth, stabilize foreign exchange rates, and the Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Communications Bank shall buy and sell foreign exchange without restriction. Splendid! This is truly the beginning of China's financial system entering the latest stage of world financial evolution. Such regulations, its position in China's future financial history, equals England's Peel's Act of 1844, and the French Bank's banknote regulations of 1848. Regarding the great achievements created in the financial history of England and France, and considering the situation, the results of the currency system bill announced by our government on the 3rd will even surpass them in the future. Since the British government formally stipulated the Bank of England's banknotes as legal tender in 1833, the basis for bank banknotes to become legal tender was established. After the Napoleonic Wars in the early 19th century, England subsequently experienced financial panic. At that time, in order to cope with the situation of cash payments, it was stipulated that Bank of England banknotes would be legal tender and replace the banknotes of other issuing banks. After implementation, significant success was achieved. After 1848, France, and after 1875, Germany, followed suit. After the European War, unprecedented changes occurred in currency systems around the world. In the past fifteen years, in European and American countries such as England, the United States, France, Italy, and Germany, the currency in circulation in the market has been the central bank's banknotes as legal tender. Except for auxiliary coins, no metal currency is used. Whether the U.S. dollar, the British pound, the French franc, the German mark, or the Italian lira was used in gold coins before the gold standard was abandoned, there were none. The currency in circulation in the market is entirely banknotes. All gold coins and gold are completely concentrated in the central bank. Except for the use of gold to offset the balance of international payments, there is no circulation of standard currency domestically. Even if cash is exchanged, the minimum amount for exchange is also stipulated, such as the exchange of French Bank banknotes, the minimum limit is still above 210,000 francs. Thus, banknotes are used domestically with gold as reserve, and gold is used externally to repay international debts. This is the guideline for the use of currency systems in recent European and American countries. In terms of its function, the currency in the market can be freely expanded and contracted, the price level can be controlled, and the national economy can also exert its effectiveness through currency management methods. It is reasonable that there are those in the world who use currency policy as a strategy for economic panic. Before the recent announcement of the bill, China's currency system was actually a chaotic monetary system. The issuance of banknotes was decentralized, and the currency in the market was still used in metal standard currency. Since the United States raised the price of silver, its weaknesses have become more obvious. Silver outflow is impossible to prevent, and there is no centralized management agency for market chips. It is clear that it cannot use currency politics to adjust financial seasons and control price level fluctuations. Now, our government has resolutely made a decisive decision to stipulate that the banknotes of the three banks are legal tender, silver standard currency is not allowed to circulate, the preparation of issuing banks is centrally managed, and it is stated that the banknotes of other banks shall be exchanged for central banknotes by the Ministry of Finance within a time limit. It is completely the same as the latest currency system in European and American countries. In the future, it will be beneficial to the development of our country's economy, and it is by no means superficial. Since the promulgation of this law, the world has praised it, but there are still two misunderstandings among the Chinese people. First, will prices rise as a result? Prices do not necessarily rise as a result of the new currency law. The surge in prices in the past two days is due to the volatility of people's hearts and the rise due to a misunderstanding of currency principles, which is often due to currency expansion. However, the government authorities have repeatedly stated that currency will never expand. If currency does not expand, prices will not rise casually. So, will prices in our country never rise in the future? Yes, they can rise and make the economy prosperous, but the reason for the rise can be due to the following two points. First, due to the reform of the currency system, market chips can obtain reasonable circulation, credit will not stagnate, and social purchasing power can be increased. Production and sales can be greatly increased, and prices will gradually return to normal. Thus, it can indirectly stimulate the development of domestic industry and commerce. Second, due to the improvement of the currency system, foreign exchange can be controlled. In recent years, our country's currency has been excessively valued due to the impact of silver prices, but this can be restored to normal. If so, the price of foreign currency will be high, the import cost of foreign goods will increase greatly, and the price of foreign goods will rise accordingly. As a result, it will be sufficient to encourage exports, reduce imports, and the international balance of payments can be adjusted. With these two reasons listed above, even if prices rise in the future, it is not the result of currency inflation, but the result of economic prosperity. In this way, the new currency law recently promulgated by our government is indeed beneficial to prices. Those who are terrified of the misunderstanding of currency inflation can be relieved. Second, will drastic changes occur in foreign exchange as a result? Our foreign exchange can be stabilized in the future, and the new law is sufficient to improve foreign exchange. Since August of last year, after the world silver price rose sharply, there have been two ways to determine our foreign exchange rate. First, to change with the changes in the world silver price, that is, to fluctuate around the parity price. If so, in recent years, our country's foreign exchange should fluctuate around 20 pence to 24 pence, but should not fluctuate around one shilling and five pence. Second, to break away from the world silver price and set the exchange rate by ourselves. The determination of our country's foreign exchange rate in the past year is the law. As a result, in fact, our country's foreign exchange has become the foreign exchange of a country that has abandoned the silver standard in the past year. The main cause of its changes is due to the need and supply of market drafts, or due to government control. However, in the past year, our country's foreign exchange has been very stable under the circumstance of breaking away from the silver price relationship. Anyone who is familiar with the recent year's determination methods of our country's foreign exchange, its principle, and its basis on the world gold price, and the power of foreign banks in the Shanghai market over the foreign exchange rate is known to be unavoidable. I have never heard of a powerful foreign bank praising our country's currency system policy. Under this situation, I don't think it will be difficult for me. Moreover, our government clearly ordered the Bank of China, the Central Bank, and the Communications Bank to do their best to supply foreign exchange, and there are already preparations for coping with it. Therefore, our country's foreign exchange in the future is still stable at a point suitable for our country's economy. Based on the past three or four years of changes in our country's foreign exchange, and the recent abandonment of the gold standard in the foreign exchange balance of countries, recently our country's foreign exchange may be rationally stabilized as a result. The government's new currency bill recently has no major impact on the fluctuation of the foreign exchange rate in terms of the principle of foreign exchange change. Moreover, before and after the promulgation of this bill, our country's foreign exchange has in fact broken away from the silver price and consolidated its defenses. The future situation is still the same.

Thieves in Zhabei are rampant, and robberies have occurred frequently recently. Was About to Go Off Duty

Chest and Fired

The two police chiefs were lying in ambush on the side of the road, and when they saw that Tang was injured and fell to the ground, they rushed forward to chase regardless of their own safety. The thieves fired their pistols indiscriminately while fighting and fleeing.

But it Was Night

The area was all wasteland, so they were able to escape. Had Already Died

Local Court

For autopsy. In the afternoon, at about 3:00 PM, Prosecutor Xiao Jinying, accompanied by clerk Zhang Guowei, arrived to examine the body. Ministry of Communications Plans to Prevent Abuses and Rectify Broadcasting Stations

In recent years, the number of broadcasting stations in various parts of China has been increasing, and the number of people using radios has also been rising rapidly. The Ministry of Communications believes that broadcasting is of great importance to a nation's politics and culture. To ensure its proper function and prevent unexpected abuses, the Ministry is implementing strict supervision of broadcasting stations. Details are as follows:

Suspension of Issuing Licenses

The Ministry of Communications stipulates that the frequency used by broadcasting stations should be from 550 kHz to 1500 kHz, with a difference of 10 kHz between each station. In practice, permits have been issued for over ninety broadcasting stations. The Ministry believes that this frequency range is now fully allocated, and existing stations are in urgent need of reorganization. Therefore, the Ministry has suspended the issuance of any new permits.

Cracking Down on Poorly Managed Stations

The Ministry of Communications closely monitors all broadcasting stations after they are approved for establishment. Those that are poorly managed will be dealt with accordingly. Serious cases will be punished. Recently, over ten stations have been cracked down upon. Some of these stations failed to establish themselves within the prescribed time after being approved. Others had faulty equipment and failed to comply with orders to improve. Some broadcast obscene content and refused to comply with orders to be punished. Others transferred or sublet their licenses without authorization.

Auditing Broadcast Programs

Regarding the broadcasting programs of each station, the Ministry of Communications has repeatedly issued instructions on what should be broadcast and what is prohibited. For the sake of convenience, the Ministry has specially ordered each station to submit a copy of its broadcast schedule. Future changes must be reported five days in advance. The Ministry plans to thoroughly review all collected broadcast schedules and make appropriate regulations regarding the general content of broadcasting stations and the allocation of time slots.

Evaded Responsibility

From hand to wrist, the skin was completely yellowed. A rag picker caught a glimpse and screamed in terror.

—The Haining Road Police Station is now investigating—

They should know that the old licenses have now expired and cannot be used any longer.

Sudden Cold Weather: Prevent the Spread of Smallpox and Diphtheria

Those who have not been vaccinated against smallpox should be vaccinated quickly. Inject antitoxin to prevent diphtheria.

Yesterday the weather suddenly turned cold. If citizens do not take care of themselves, it will easily lead to disease. When the weather suddenly turns cold, the diseases most likely to spread are smallpox and diphtheria. As a preventative measure, citizens who have not been vaccinated against smallpox should go to the health offices in each district of the city and designated vaccination branches to get vaccinated to avoid contracting smallpox. To prevent diphtheria, parents should take children under the age of fifteen to hospitals or reputable doctors to inject antitoxin during this cold season when it is easy to spread. Injection can prevent infection. If one child in the family has diphtheria, the other children should be kept away from the sick child to prevent infection. These are important for our health, and it is hoped that citizens will pay attention, take preventative measures as soon as possible, and reduce the possibility of these diseases occurring.

Municipal Public Security Bureau: Tea House Registration Deadline Today

Registration of Employment Agencies to be Implemented Next Month

The registration of tea houses by the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which began on July 1, was originally scheduled to end at the end of last month. However, in order to avoid omissions, the Bureau extended the deadline by one week, setting today (7th) as the official deadline. Since April, approximately 1,400 tea houses have applied for registration, of which over 700 have been approved and over 600 have been rejected. Once the registration is officially closed, those whose registration has been rejected will be ordered to close down. Furthermore, after the Bureau decided to rectify the employment agencies in the city starting on the 1st of this month, it has been sending personnel to investigate the internal situation of each agency in recent days, looking for any cases of abduction or other illegal activities. Starting next month, it will conduct the registration of each agency and limit the establishment of new agencies in the future, in order to thoroughly eliminate the various illegal activities of employment agencies in the past.

It is now actively preparing. In recent years, the company has been working hard to produce new products, and various tonics have shown significant efficacy. The establishment of a new branch in the western district is also part of its business development. It is reported that the branch will officially open within this month.

Municipal Federation Petitions the Municipal Government to Ban Dance Halls

The Municipal Government should strictly prohibit the nightly revelry and dancing that squanders the ambition of youth in order to salvage decent morals.

Dagong News: The Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation received letters from the 7th, 18th, 27th, 35th, 38th, and other branches, stating that the abnormal development of dance halls in the city attracts young men and women, not only consuming huge amounts of money and the ambitions of young people, but also fostering an atmosphere of decadence. At a time when the international situation is becoming increasingly tense, our young people should be especially vigilant about their future and work together to overcome national difficulties. After approving the letter, the Citizens' Federation petitioned the Municipal Government yesterday to implement a ban. The original petition is recorded below. We petition for a ban on the operation of dance halls in order to salvage decent morals and maintain public interests. According to the letters from the 7th, 18th, 27th, 35th, 38th, and other branches of this federation, the operation of dance halls has developed abnormally in recent years, like bamboo shoots after a spring rain. Every night, they attract young men and women, reveling and dancing throughout the night, not only causing decent young people to squander their ambitions and consume huge amounts of money, but also fostering an atmosphere of decadence. The Ministry of Education has explicitly banned middle school and above students from participating in dancing, which shows that dancing is an indecent form of entertainment. At a time when the international situation is becoming increasingly tense, patriotic young people should be especially vigilant about their future and work together to overcome national difficulties. Today, dance halls use licentious entertainment to harm the bodies and minds of young people, which is intolerable to the society and the nation. Therefore, we specially jointly request that the authorities be petitioned to promptly ban them. After careful discussion by the fifth executive committee of this federation, it was said that proper dancing is inherently a form of physical exercise and should not be criticized too harshly. However, today's dance halls in the city are aimed at making profits, and their extravagance has reached the extreme, harming good morals and being nothing short of a trap for young people. Moreover, at a time when national crisis is pressing and disasters are severe in various places, this display of extravagant and licentious joy is even more heartbreaking. If it is not banned, it will directly harm the bodies and minds of young people and destroy the lifeblood of the country. The harm caused will also affect public interests. Look at today's rampant theft cases. Investigating the reasons, it is because these people live dissolute lives and indulge in extravagance and debauchery. Therefore, tolerating the existence of dance halls is sufficient to cause great chaos and increase social unrest. Therefore, it was decided to request that the authorities promptly order a ban. Even if there are practical difficulties and it is inconvenient to take severe measures at once, in the view of this federation, the following two restrictions should be implemented first: (1) The authorities should stop issuing licenses for the operation of new dance halls in the future; (2) The operating hours of dance halls should not exceed 12 p.m. in order to gradually achieve the goal of banning them. The matter concerns social stability and public interests, so we specially petition your government to approve and implement a ban in order to correct good morals and maintain public interests. We are deeply grateful. Sincerely presented to Wu, the Mayor of the Shanghai Municipal Government (The wording of the letter to the Public Works Department is omitted).

Page 12

Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company: Passenger Cars Fitted with Wood-Burning Generators as a Substitute for Oil, Formal Contract Signed with Zhongming Factory

According to customs reports, the annual excess of gasoline imports exceeds 100 million yuan. At present, gasoline prices have risen by two-tenths, so the excess of imports will also increase by two-tenths. Patriotic people are all thinking of ways to stop this leak. Therefore, the wood-burning generator invented by Tang Shenming has been noticed and valued by the Chinese people. The Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company test-fitted it to a large passenger car a month ago and ran it between Shanghai and Changshu. The results were not bad. Its speed is slightly lower than gasoline, but it can still travel at up to 40 miles per hour. According to the company's regulations, such a speed is not required. If the speed can be maintained between 25 miles per hour and 30 miles per hour, it is sufficient for the application of long-distance bus companies. If the cost of consumption is considered, it can save two-thirds of the cost. Therefore, the general manager of the Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company, Wang Xiaolai, and the manager, Zhu Kaichou, were concerned about the increasing price of gasoline and felt that it had an impact on the company's expenditure. Seeing that the test use of the wood-burning generator by the company was still good, they resolutely decided to convert all of the large passenger cars to wood-burning generators and formally signed a contract with the Zhongming Factory at the Dengtuomo Hotel on the 5th of this month, setting a completion date of three months. Those present at the time included the general manager of the Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company, Wang Xiaolai, the manager, Zhu Kaichou, the director of the engineering department, Wang Zongshan, the director of the vehicle department, Wu Zhongyi, and others. The representatives of the Zhongming Factory included the general manager, Fan Zhengbo, the engineer, Tang Zhongming, and others. Everyone parted on good terms.

Tomorrow's Youth Concert at the Lyceum Theatre

During the last meeting convened by the Municipal Council's Music Committee, it was decided to hold two special concerts suitable for young people within this year, and the dates were agreed upon as November 8th and December 20th. Therefore, tomorrow is the date of the first special youth concert, still at the Lyceum Theatre, at 5:15 PM. The purpose of holding such youth concerts is not only to give young people ninety minutes of musical enjoyment but also to develop their musical appreciation while listening to music. Therefore, the Municipal Council Orchestra has put a lot of effort into selecting the program for this concert. The conductor will explain the structure, musical themes, and advantages of each piece to the audience before the performance, with "The Making of Music and its Main Forms" as the general title of the first youth concert lecture. During the lecture, the orchestra conductor will strive to avoid all advanced artistic terms and will not involve the analysis of the highest forms of music. He will only use simple language and basic theory to explain how composers combine thoughts and sounds in each piece. Furthermore, to help beginners understand various musical rhythms, several dances from different countries have been specially selected as the main body of this program, so that beginners can understand and appreciate them intuitively.

Opium Addict Loses Opium Cessation License

Whether to Investigate Unpurchased Official Soil

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that Shanghai County Magistrate Ye Zhendong has drafted two measures regarding how to handle the loss of opium cessation licenses by opium addicts and has submitted them to the Civil Affairs Department for review. It is now heard that the provincial government has revised the measures as follows: (1) If an opium addict loses his opium cessation license and takes the initiative to report it for reissuance before it is discovered, in addition to handling it in accordance with Article 11 of the Jiangsu Province Regulations on the Prohibition of Opium Addiction within a Specified Period, it should also be investigated whether he has failed to purchase official soil and should be severely punished according to law. (2) If an opium addict loses his opium cessation license and does not report it for reissuance according to law, after it is discovered, in addition to handling it in accordance with Article 11 of the Jiangsu Province Regulations on the Prohibition of Opium Addiction within a Specified Period, it should also be investigated whether he has failed to purchase official soil and should be punished accordingly. If someone, after obtaining an opium cessation license, has not purchased official soil according to the regulations and falsely claims to have lost the license in the hope of secretly purchasing private goods, he will be dealt with as a private addict. The above two measures have been ordered by the Jiangsu Provincial Government to be followed.

Opium Addicts in Longhua on Hunger Strike

Punish the Leaders to End the Disturbance - Zhang Houyuan from Ningbo, a coppersmith, and Zhou Zhiliang, a peddler, were both deeply addicted to opium. Knowing that the prohibition of opium was strict and they were unable to register, they voluntarily went to the Longhua Shanghai Municipal Criminal Addiction Rehabilitation Hospital for treatment. In order to eliminate opium addiction and encourage voluntary cessation, the hospital admitted them. However, these inmates usually did not comply with the hospital rules, and recently incited other inmates to demand a complete hunger strike on various pretexts. The hospital director's persuasion was ineffective, so he sent the two leading opium addicts, Zhang and Zhou, to the Caojing Police Station to inquire about the situation and transfer them to the headquarters for punishment according to the law. At this point, the remaining inmates realized they had been deceived and declared to the director that they had been completely blindly following and begged for leniency. The director, considering their ignorance, agreed to lenient treatment, and the hunger strike ended.

Alas, a Laborer - Crushed to Death by Machine

Sun Weifa from Siyang, 34 years old, living at 25 Xinhua Lane, Meizhou Road, Pingliang Road, was a laborer at the No. 1 Iron Factory at the corner of Linqing Road No. 40. Last night at 11:00 PM, Sun was on the night shift when his feet were suddenly caught in the machine and crushed, with blood and flesh mixed together, rendering him unconscious. His companions immediately stopped the machine and tried to rescue Sun, rushing him to Sacred Heart Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he soon died.

Woman Abuses Apprentice to Death

Wang Guisheng, a boy from Jiangbei, 15 years old, was recommended this spring to work as an apprentice in a barbershop opened by a Mr. Chen in Wusong Town. Chen's wife was extremely fierce and often used corporal punishment, causing Wang unbearable suffering. A few days ago, he was severely beaten again over a trivial matter. Neighbors, feeling injustice, reported it to the police, who detained Chen in the police station. The injured boy was sent to the Wusong Health Hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, Wang was already unconscious upon arrival at the hospital. Despite the doctor's efforts to save him, his injuries were too severe and could not be reversed, and he soon died. Yesterday afternoon, the local guarantor reported it to the local court for an autopsy. Inspector Xiao and coroner Shen from the Prosecutor's Office arrived at the hospital and confirmed that Wang Guisheng died as a result of injuries. They filled out the form and ordered the coffin to be prepared, and the police station would transfer Chen to the case for interrogation and legal action.

Laborer Dies in Car Accident

Jiangbei native Shi Jinsu, a laborer, 24 years old, residing at No. 380 Xie Family Lane, Jufu Road, French Concession, at around 6:00 PM on the 5th, Shi encountered a truck F1051 from the French Concession, driven by driver Hong Chunyuan (32 years old, from Ningbo, residing at No. 16 Tongfeng Lane, Xujiahui Road), carrying soil from north to south at the intersection of Route Lafayette and Rue Pichon. Shi, in order to hitch a ride, jumped onto the truck. When the truck reached the front of the private residence of the Japanese Minister near the intersection of Route Dollfus and Route Tenant de la Tour, Shi had reached his destination. Without waiting for the truck to stop, he jumped off the truck and fell backward due to instability, causing him to break the back of his head, with blood flowing like a stream, rendering him unconscious. A patrol officer discovered this and sent Shi to Guangci Hospital. The truck driver was taken to the police station for investigation. Shi died at 2:00 AM that night due to severe head injuries. The hospital notified the police station, who sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuantang autopsy site. The deceased had no family. At noon yesterday, Wang Ren, a prosecutor from the Special Second Court, along with a forensic doctor and clerk, arrived at the site. After the autopsy, it was confirmed that the deceased died as a result of falling while jumping off the truck. The official interrogated the witness, truck driver Hong Chunyuan, and laborer Yang Bingcheng, regarding the circumstances of the accident. The official ordered the body to be transported to Tongren Fuyuantang for burial, pending family recognition.

At 10:50 AM yesterday (the 6th), a fire broke out at the residence of the Wu family at No. 11, Lane 280, Binlang Road, Conneau Road, Shanghai West, due to carelessness while cooking. The fire quickly spread through the roof. Firefighters arrived with water tankers and extinguished the fire at 12:00 PM. The fire spread to the neighboring houses at No. 40 and No. 41, destroying a total of three buildings.

More than 1,000 Winners Last Month

The value of the coupon ranges from (2,000 yuan), (1,000 yuan), (50 yuan), (5 yuan), (1 yuan), etc., with the lowest being able to get a bottle of Butterfly Cream or Toothpaste. Since its release, in less than a month, there have been more than a thousand winners. All coupons worth 5 yuan or more are signed and stamped by the winners and redeemed directly from the Shanghai Home Industry Cooperative. Coupons worth less than 5 yuan and Butterfly Cream and Toothpaste can be redeemed by managers in various ports. In order to demonstrate its credibility, the cooperative will collect the names and addresses of winners from various ports and publish them. This coupon can be found in any Invincible Brand Toothpaste or Butterfly Cream and is very easy to obtain. When packaging, an average of one coupon is placed in every ten bottles of Butterfly Cream or ten tubes of Toothpaste, but the boxes are mixed up, so lucky people can win continuously.

Paintings by Famous Painter He Tianjian

Mr. He Tianjian, who also calls himself "A Literatus at the Hundred-Foot Building," is deeply rooted in the Northern Song Dynasty. He has reportedly traveled to famous mountains and rivers, which explains the magic in his brushstrokes and his imposing style. Everything he sees is expressed through his hands, and everything he holds in his heart is conveyed through his brush, so he has a unique style that does not rigidly adhere to one school but has his own divine touch. The recent National Painting Monthly is hosted by him, and his lofty style is evident. People at sea, both familiar and unfamiliar, know that his calligraphy and paintings are precious and not easy to obtain. It is said that Mr. He does not want to keep his works secret and is willing to share them with enthusiasts. Here are some painting examples to indicate his prices. For his freehand paintings, a full sheet of four to six feet costs 14 yuan per foot, and eight to twelve feet costs 24 yuan per foot. Semi-detailed paintings cost 20 yuan per foot, and detailed paintings cost 30 yuan per foot. Larger works are priced accordingly. Vertical scrolls and screen strips are calculated at 90% of the full sheet price. Other items have separate price lists. Major stationery stores in this city and other locations can accept orders.

China National Products Trading Company is funded by major figures in domestic industry. Recently, the company has newly invented a kind of fine art scented soap. It can be called a high-quality domestic industrial product comparable to imported products. Other large companies and foreign and miscellaneous grocery stores also sell it.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather around Shandong is clear and obstructed, with strong northwest to northeast winds of varying degrees. The Yangtze River Basin is cloudy and cold, sometimes turning overcast, with gentle north to east winds of varying degrees. The East China Sea and Taiwan have strong northeast monsoon season winds. There is rain in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 63.9 degrees and the lowest was 50.0 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 59.9 degrees and the lowest was 52.0 degrees.
